tasya madhye sthitaṃ śeṣaṃ sahasra phaṇiśobhitam || 23 ||  
  
tasya madhye sthitaṃ devaṃ śivasūryannamonamaḥ |  
  
|| dvādaśādityau ||  
  
aruṇāsūryanāmā ca sahasrāṃśustathāpahe |  
dātāra viśvaparjanyāṃ tvaṣṭrāmitrasyavāsavaḥ || 24 ||  
  
ete dvādaśasūryāśca dvibhujāvaradāmbujāḥ |  
  
p. 67)  
  
dvādaśādityaśaktiḥ ||  
  
ubhaḥ prabhāśca sabhyāśca prajñā medhā ca mālini |  
sāvitrī caiva gāyatri śrīpratīkāntimīritā |  
ete dvādaśasūryāṇāṃ śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ || 25 ||  
  
|| candran ||  
  
śvetavarṇandvinetrañca śvetapadmoparisthitam |  
dvibhujaṃ kumudopetaṃ śvetavastreṇa veṣṭitam ||  
  
sarvairābharaṇaibhūṣyairmuktādāmairalaṅkṛtam |  
kirīṭamakuṭañcaiva prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam || 1 ||  
  
kṛttikā dakṣiṇe pārśve rohiṇiṃ vāmapārśvake |  
  
|| candran ||  
  
citrasiṃhāsanāsīnaṃ kundasphaṭikasannibham |  
prabhāmaṇḍala saṃyuktā dvibhujāñcadvināsikam ||  
  
āsīno vā sthito vā'pi kumudaḥ prajalākaraḥ |  
tasya dakṣiṇa digbhāge rohiṇī dvibhujānvitam || 2 ||  
  
sanaṅkuranibhābhāsvat rājīvasamalocanaḥ |  
  
punaḥ-  
  
punaḥ-  
  
gokṣīradhavalākāraṃ dvibhujañca dvinetrakam ||  
  
raśmimaṇḍalasaṃyuktaṃ vaiḍūryamakuṭānvitam |  
  
p. 70)  
  
rohiṇīsahitaṃ candraṃ dhyāyet kumudahastakam |  
arcanasya tataḥ kṛtvā netranyāsārghyamarcayet || 3 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
ekavaktrandvinetrañca śvetavarṇañcaturbhujam |  
śvetapadmāsanāsīnaṃ śvetavastrasudhāriṇam ||  
  
śvetagandhākṣatañcaivā jājīpuṣpa sudhāriṇam |  
muktāhāravibhūṣañca śvetābjañca dvihastakam ||  
  
dhanurbāṇadvihastañca saptāśvarathavāhanam |  
kṛttikārohiṇīñcaivā dvipārśve śyāmavarṇakam ||  
  
śītālitalamevantu ṣoḍaśaḥ kalasaṃyutam |  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ candrarūpāyate namaḥ || 4 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
dvibhujaṃ kumudañcaiva prabhāmaṇḍalaśobhitam |  
ekavaktrandvinetrañca hāramuktāmaṇiṃ yathā |  
jājicampakamālāyā vaktrasyopari saṃsthitam ||  
  
śvetapadmāsanañcaiva dviśaktiñca dvipārśvakam |  
śvetavastradharañcaiva sarvālaṅkāraśobhitam ||  
ṣoḍaśaḥ kalaśaṃ yuktaṃ pūrṇacandrasvarūpakam || 5 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
svarṇa divyarathārūḍhaṃ rathasaptāśva pītakam |  
śvetavarṇadhvajaṃ rajjuṃ śvetachatreṇa cāmaram ||  
  
p. 71)  
  
śvetavastrairalaṅkāraṃ tanmadhye padmapīṭhakam |  
pīṭhamadhye suvṛktañca tanmadhye candrarūpiṇam || 6 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
ekavaktraṃ dvihastābjaṃ dvinetraṃ śāntarūpiṇam |  
navaratnakirīṭañca svarṇamābharaṇānvitam ||  
  
śrī gandhantilakañcaiva puṣpamālāsucāpakam |  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ candrarūpāya te namaḥ || 7 ||  
  
|| brahmā dhyānam ||  
  
pītaṃ pīnaṃ caturbāhuṃ brahmāṇañcaturānanam |  
haṃsayānañca bibhrāṇaṃ daṇḍākṣassṛkkamaṇḍalum || 1 ||  
  
brahmā caturmukhaḥ pītā caturdordaṇḍamaṇḍitaḥ |  
srukdaṇḍākṣakuśopetā sūryamaṇḍalamadhyagaḥ ||  
  
tatraivordhvadiśānāthaṃ proktākārantathaiva ca |  
kamaṇḍalvakṣamālāñca kuśadaṇḍadharaṃ bhaje || 2 ||  
  
adho digadhipaṃ kāntaṃ pītavastraṃ śriyānvitam |  
caturvaktre bhujāṣṭau ca śaktiñca japamālayoḥ ||  
  
kuśadaṇḍakapālañca jñānamudrāñca postakam |  
likhitaṃ savyahastena ṛṣīṇāñca prapūjayet || 3 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
śvetavarṇa svarūpantu caturvaktrañcaturbhujam |  
  
p. 72)  
  
daṇḍañca sarvamevantu japamālākamaṇḍalum |  
yogapīṭhāsanañcaiva aṣṭanetrantathaiva ca ||  
  
ṛṣipuṣpāñjaliñcaiva caturvedādikantathā |  
aṣṭādaśapurāṇañca ṣaṭśāstrakalavijñakam ||  
  
mīmāṃsayogaśāstrañca bhārati jihvayānvitam |  
navaratnakirīṭañca vajramābharaṇantathā ||  
  
śvetavastrasamāyuktaṃ bāhuḥ yajñopavītinam |  
devāsuramahaṃvande ravimaṇḍalasaṃyutam || 4 ||  
  
ityevaṃ brahmarūpantu dhyātvā mantreṇa pūjayet |  
  
punaḥ-  
  
vedaśāstrapurāṇañca bhāṣitaṃ pūrvavaktrake ||  
  
devāsura-ṛṣīn vande bhāṣitaṃ dakṣiṇena ca |  
likhitā sṛṣṭimevantu vaktramuttarameva ca ||   
  
parameśvara pādābjaṃ puṣpāñjali samaprabham |  
paścimābhimukhandevaṃ dhyātvā brahmasvarūpakam || 5 ||  
  
|| viṣṇu dhyānam ||  
  
viṣṇuścaturbhujo māliṃ śaṅkhacakragadābjadhṛk |  
nīlāmbudapratīkāśaṃ somamaṇḍalakeśavā || 1 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
paścāsuvarṇa varṇābhaṃ raktāsyaṃ raktanetrakam |  
  
p. 73)  
  
pāṇipādasukhodvāhaṃ śukapiñcāmbaraṃ harim |  
śrī viṣṇupraṇavātmānaṃ kirīṭaṃ vaktrasannibham ||  
  
praṇālamupavītañca śrīvatsāṅgaṃ caturbhujam |  
śaṅkhacakrāvatārañca kalābhayavalambakam || 2 ||  
  
sa eva paramātmānaṃ dhyātvā viṣṇusvarūpakam |  
anantaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ phaṇādaśaśatairyutam || 3 ||  
  
vidyuddhāma pratīkāśaṃ kūrmārūḍhaṃ kṛtāñjalim |  
anantaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ ekavaktrañcaturbhujam ||  
  
dhanurbāṇasamāyuktaṃ kirīṭamakuṭojjvalam |  
hārakeyūra saṃyuktadvinetraṃ raktavāsasam ||  
  
śaṅkhacakradharandevaṃ somamaṇḍalarakṣakam |  
surāsurakṛtaṃ vande puṣpāñjali samaprabham || 4 ||  
  
evaṃ viṣṇusvarūpantu dhyātvā mantreṇa pūjayet |  
nīlavarṇasvarūpantu ekavaktrañcaturbhujam ||  
  
śaṅkhacakrāvatārañcā hemāṅgulyādibhūṣaṇam |  
vakṣasthalenakañcaiva lakṣmīndivyasvarūpakam ||  
  
āliṅganena hastāñca abhayandakṣiṇe kare |  
pītāmbaropavītañca svarṇaratna kirīṭakam || 5 ||  
  
p. 74)  
  
lakṣmīnārāyaṇañcaivā dhyātvā mantreṇa pūjayet |  
  
|| rāmar ||  
  
bālārkadyuti sannibhaṃ raghuvaraṃ sītāpate paścime  
tiṣṭhantinnavaratna citramakuṭaṃ hārollasadvakṣasam |  
śvetacchatradharaṃ suvarṇakaṭakaṃ svarṇāṅkarālaṅkṛtaṃ  
devaṃ lakṣmaṇa ūrmilāsahavaraṃ vandesumitrāsutam || 6 ||  
  
maṇḍavyākelilolaṃ maṇimayamakuṭaṃ maṅgalānānnivāsaṃ   
tālībṛndaṃ dadhānaṃ śaśinibhavadanaṃ padmapatrāyatākṣam |  
bhaktānāṃ pārijātaṃ bhavabhayaharaṃ rāmavāme niviṣṭhaṃ   
ratnorvairmaṇḍitāṅgaṃ bharatamunikulayīśvaraṃ cintayāmi || 7 ||  
  
śatrughnandīrghabāhuṃ vividhamaṇigaṇālaṅkṛtāṅgaṃ bhaje'haṃ   
sītāhāṭaka sannibhāṃ śaśimukhāṃ hārāvalī śobhitām |  
kastūrīvanasārabhūṣitakucāṃ hemāmbarālaṅkṛtāṃ   
ratnonmīlita kuṇḍalāṃ raghuvarāsyāṃkaimudārasthitām || 8 ||  
  
devīṃ mātaramāśrayāmi jagatāṃ sarvārthasiddhi pradāṃ ||  
  
rāmasyāgre pavananamamalaṃ hemayajñopavītam ||  
sītāśokāgnikālāmbudaśubhaharaṃ divyavaktrojjvalāṅgaṃ  
bhaktānāṃ pārijātaṃ nicarakulasaṃhārakālāgnirudram |  
  
p. 75)  
  
dhyāyedgāṅgeya varṇaṃ pramudita vadanaṃ postakaṃ sandadhānam || 9 ||  
  
|| vīrarāmar ||  
  
hastāyudhe daśāsyaṃ tribhulataviṣamaṃ vāmahastena cāpaṃ  
bhūmau ṣaṭṭaṃ viṣṭaśyatiṣṭhannijakarakadhṛtaṃ bhrāmayanbāṇamekam |  
āratnopāntanetraṃ śaradalivapuṣaṃ koṭisūryaṃ prakāśaṃ   
vīraśrībaddharāgaṃ tridaśapatinutaṃ pātu māṃ vīrarāmam || 10 ||  
  
vīrarāmar  
  
dorbhiḥ khaḍgaṃ triśūlaṃ ḍamarukadhanuṃ candrabāṇaṃ kuṭhāraṃ   
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ kṛpāṇaṃ halamusalagataṃ piṇḍibālañca kheṭam |  
udyadvahniñca muṣṭiṃ abhayavarakaraṃ śyāṅkuśaṃ vāmabhāge  
vande rāmaṃ triṇetraṃ mama duritaharaṃ pātu māṃ vīrarāmam || 11 ||  
  
rāmaṃ ratnakirīṭa kuṇḍaladharaṃ vaktraṃ śaśībiṃbakaṃ   
vastraṃ hemasudhāvaraṃ karacatuścakraṃ dhanurbāṇakam |  
śaṅkhaṃ jājisupuṣpavanadalaṃ mālāyavakṣasthalaṃ  
śatrughnaṃ bharataṃ salakṣaṇayutaṃ sītātha vāme sthitam || 12 ||  
  
śrī gandhaṃ anulepanañca tilakaṃ bhaktipriyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ  
sarvālaṅkṛtaśobhitaṃ surapatiṃ rāmaṃ bhaje'haṃ bhaje |  
  
|| viṣṇuṣoḍaśanāmam ||  
  
p. 76)  
  
auṣadhañcintayedviṣṇo bhojanena janārdanam |  
śayane padmanābhañca saṃyogena prajāpati ||  
  
nārāyaṇodya kālañca śrīdharaṃ prayasaṃgame |  
saṃgrāme cakriṇañcaiva prabhāte śatruvikramaḥ ||  
  
dusvapne smaragovindaṃ bhībhatso madhusūdanam |  
kānane narasiṃhañca parvate raghunandanam ||  
  
jalamadhye varāhasya pāvake jalaśāyane |  
pravāhe vāmanañcaiva sarvakāryeṣu mādhavam ||  
  
ete ṣoḍaśanāmāni trisandhyāṃ yaḥ paṭhennaraḥ |  
sarvabhūtabhayannāsti saṃgrāme vijayī bhavet || 13 ||  
  
|| vīrabhadradhyānam ||  
  
vīrabhadrantriṇetrañca nīlarūpaṃ caturbhujam |  
khaḍgañca kheṭakañcaiva pūrvahastāntare tathā ||  
  
pārśvahastāntare caiva bāṇaṃ vai kārmukantathā |  
raktavastrasamāyuktaṃ vīranūpurabhūṣitam ||  
  
yajñopavītasaṃyuktaṃ itarejāhnavītaram |  
karṇe girisamāyuktaṃ śiromālāvibhūṣitam ||  
  
rājasaṃ ugranetraṃ ca bhīmadaṃṣṭraṃ tathaiva ca |  
  
p. 77)  
  
susthitaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ vāmapādantu kuñcitam ||  
  
pādannūpurasaṃyuktaṃ channavīrasamanvitam |  
ityukte vīrabhadreva dvividhaṃ bhojamucyate || 1 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
triṇetraṃ śyāmavarṇañca śiromālā vibhūṣitam |  
jaṭāmakuṭasaṃyuktaṃ jāhnavī candrasaṃyutam ||  
  
āsthānasatsayetpādaṃ dakṣapādantu lambitam |  
vāmapādaṃ vilambañca samadehaṃ prakalpayet ||   
  
sarvabhāgaddhṛdañcaiva khaḍgañca hariṇantathā |  
vāmapārśve tu haste tu kheṭakaṃ paraśuntathā ||  
  
savyapāde ca pārśve tu dakṣañcaiva prajāpatim |  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 2 ||  
  
bhogañca vividhaṃ proktaṃ vīrañca vividhaṃ śṛṇu |  
  
punaḥ-  
  
tadbhujāṣṭasamāyuktaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ||  
  
śūlaṃ khaḍgañca bāṇañca hariṇīṃ dakṣapārśvake |  
kapālakheṭakañcaiva pāśamaṅkuśavāmake || 3 ||  
  
dhyānakaṃ vīradevañca trividhaṃ cocyate kramāt |  
  
punaḥ-  
  
śvetākāramaśeṣa bhūṣaṇadharaṃ vinyastavīṇādharaṃ   
ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgādharaṃ karayuge śārdūlacarmāmbaram |  
  
p. 78)  
  
ardhonīla na locanaṃ triyayutaṃ maulī jaṭābandhanaṃ   
vande sannatavīrabhadracaraṇaṃ ambhoruhaṃ pāhimām || 4 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
rudrāṃ raudrāvatāraṃ hutavahanayanaṃ ūrdhvakeśaṃ sudaṃṣṭraṃ  
bhīmaṃ bhīmāṅgarūpaṃ ghṛṇighṛṇininadaṃ jvālamālāvṛtāṅgam |  
bhūtapretādhināthaṃ kathanakalahataṃ khaḍgapātrevahantaṃ   
vande lokaikanāthaṃ tripuradahanaṃdaṃ śyāmalaṃ vīrabhadram || 5 ||  
  
punaḥ-  
  
bālāpaṭṭa samajjvalaṃ ghanavaraṃ pādābjaye nūpuraṃ  
nānādeva samanvitaṃ śaśidharaṃ nāgendrabhūṣojjvalam |  
vande vāruṇavīrabhadramabhayaṃ tvaṃ vīradevaṃ bhaje || 6 ||  
  
|| viśvahṛdayam ||  
  
anajadaṇḍakamaṇḍulumekhalāṃ rucirapāvana vāma na mūrtaye |  
nitarajagatraya jīvakaraparai nigamavāvān paṭavaivaṭave namaḥ || 7 ||  
  
|| śarabham ||  
  
aghora śarabhañcaivā ekavaktraṃ triṇetrakam |  
nīlavarṇasamākhyātaṃ ṣoḍaśāstaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
khaḍgantriśūlaṃ ḍamaruṃ gadā cakrāṅkuśantathā |  
bāṇāgniñca tataḥ kṛtvā savya pārśvena hastayoḥ ||  
  
p. 79)  
  
kapālaṃ paraśuṃ daṇḍaṃ pāśaghaṇṭadhanurdharam |  
khaṭvābhaṃ nāgapāśañca vāmapārśvena hastakam ||  
  
śirojaṭasamāyuktaṃ bhasmaṃ sarvāṅgadhūlitam |  
śiraḥ kiṅkiṇimālāyāṃ sarvayajñopavītinam ||  
  
raktavastreṇa saṃyuktaṃ raktaśchatra dhvajantathā |  
vikāramaṭṭahāsañca saptakoṭyāgaṇāśriyam || 8 ||  
  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ dhyātvā śarabhaṃ namāmyaham |  
  
|| maṇidhyānam ||  
  
ghaṇṭañca vividhaṃ proktaṃ pramāṇaṃ ṣaṭdaśantathā |  
bhānudvayonnatāṅgulyaṃ ghaṇṭārūpāya te namaḥ || 1 ||  
  
|| ghaṇṭapramāṇam ||  
  
nālasyonnatabhānuśca vasudeva suvṛktakam |  
nālāgre daṇḍamevantu rudrāṅgulasamanvitam || 2 ||  
  
bhūtasaṃkhyā ca daṇḍāgre pramāṇaṃ ghaṇṭarūpakam |  
nālandivākarañcaiva daṇḍañcaiva maheśvaram ||  
  
daṇḍāgreṇa triśūlañca ghaṇṭānāda sarasvati |  
ityetadghaṇṭadevānāṃ arcayettu namonamaḥ || 3 ||  
  
p. 80)  
  
|| vṛṣabhaśakti ||  
  
jvālādhvakeśi sudaṃṣṭradvinetrinaṃ sādvayaṃ vediśacakracāpi |  
bāṇañca paścādvarābhayaiśca vṛṣaśca śakti vṛṣadevavāme || 4 ||  
  
vṛṣabhaṃ śvetavarṇantu tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaṃ mahābalam |  
divyarūpasvalāvaṇyaṃ taptakāñcana sannibham ||  
  
vedarūpañcatuṣpādaṃ agnirūpantu śṛṅgakam |  
ādityaścandranetraśca mukhaṃ rudrastathaiva ca ||  
  
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca rūpaṃ vṛṣabhamucyate |  
īśvaro valayañcaivā sarvavedamayaṃ vṛṣam || 5 ||  
  
|| śayanavṛṣabham ||  
  
kṛtatretāyugañcaivā dvāpare pādajampuṭam |  
kaliyugeneka pādantu bahuśaiva vimokṣatam ||  
  
dharmadeva samākhyātaṃ paścimābhimukhantathā |  
śayanaṃ kṛtvā tu dharmajñaṃ śivavāhanamucyate || 6 ||  
  
|| vṛṣabham ||  
  
pratyaṅgāśasthitaṃ tryakṣaṃ vṛṣañca dhavalākṛtim |  
sākṣādharma svarūpañca parameśvaravāhanam || 7 ||  
  
vṛṣo vṛṣākṛtītryaikṣo rudraikāgatamānasaḥ |  
  
p. 81)  
  
sākṣāddharma svarūpañca śuddhasphaṭika nirmalaḥ || 8 ||  
  
divyaliṅgabalidevatāḥ   
  
|| aṣṭamūrti varṇabhedam ||  
  
devīkantu bhavātīnāṃ indrādīnāntu mānuṣam |  
bhūtādīnāṃ svayambhūtaṃ āruṣaṃ parivārakaiḥ ||  
  
sarodruvādibāṇañca vidyeśānāntu divyakam |  
yakṣādirākṣasaṃ liṅgaṃ baliṃ dadyāt prakīrtitāḥ || 9 ||  
  
|| devaliṅgabalidevatai ||  
  
aṣṭamūrtivarṇabhbhedāḥ   
  
bhavaśarvastathaiśānaḥ paśupatyugrameva ca |  
bhīmo rudro mahādevo ityaṣṭamūrtayastathā || 10 ||  
  
bhavasya pītavarṇañcā śarvāya rajanī tathā |  
īśānaṃ śvetavarṇañca paśupat śyāmavarṇakam ||  
  
rudrāya mekhavarṇañca hariṇīmugrarūpakam |  
sphaṭikañca mahābhīmaṃ mahādevāya ratnakam || 11 ||  
  
ityevamaṣṭamūrtiñca varṇabhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
  
|| devīkaliṅgabalidhyānam ||  
  
abhayaṃ varadañcaiva pāśāṅkuśa caturbhujam |  
triṇemekhavarṇañca dvipādañcaiva nūpuram ||  
  
jaṭāmakuṭasaṃyuktaṃ aṣṭamūrtisvarūpakam |  
  
p. 82)  
  
devīkākhyantu liṅgañca balindadyātprakīrtitāḥ || 12 ||  
  
|| mānuṣaliṅgabalidhyānam ||  
  
indrāgniśca yamañcaiva nir-ṛtīvaruṇantathā |  
vāyusomastathaiśānyo brahmāviṣṇuścalokayan ||  
  
mānuṣaṃ liṅgavatkṛtvā lokapālān balintathā |  
tatpūrve dhānyavarṇantu tadbaliṃ nikṣipettathā || 13 ||  
  
|| svayambhūliṅgadhyānam ||  
  
saṃvarto raktavarṇañca pūrvadigdalameva ca |  
śyāmaraktaṃ śvetavarṇaṃ agnito carakantathā ||  
  
kunḍodarasya kṛṣṇañca dale dakṣiṇameva ca |  
pītañca dīrghakāyau ca nir-ṛtīśca dale tathā ||  
  
hrasvapādamiti śyāmaṃ paścime dalasaṃyutam |  
atiraktañca siṃhañca vāyavyadalameva ca ||   
  
nīlaṃ gajamukhañcaiva uttare dalasaṃyutam |  
aiśānyāṃ pramukhañcaiva mekha varṇamiti smṛtam || 14 ||  
  
vṛṣāṣṭavarṇamityuktaṃ tattaddigdalameva ca |  
  
|| balidhyānam ||  
  
ugrarūpasamāyuktaṃ dvibhujañca dvipādakam |  
  
p. 83)  
  
daṇḍahastaṃ tathā savye kapālaṃ vāmahastake |  
dvinetraraktavarṇañca bhūtarūpamiti smṛtam || 15 ||  
  
aṣṭabhūtamitikhyātaṃ svāyambhuvabaliṃ kṣipet |  
  
|| ṛṣiliṅgabalidhyānam ||  
  
madhyahārañca hārāyāṃ vṛṣabhādi pradakṣiṇam |  
vṛṣabhaṃ pūrvadigbhāge āgneyyāṃ pāvakantathā ||  
  
mātṝṇāṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge vīravighneśa nai-ṛte |  
paścime skandamevantu jyeṣṭhādi vāyudigdale ||  
  
durgāśca uttare caiva aiśānye caṇḍarūpakam |  
bhāskarasya mukhaṃ pūrvaṃ aiśānye krapayastathā ||  
  
āgneyaśca tataḥ kṛtvā pavamānālayantathā |  
parivārālayaṃ sarvaṃ sarva bāhyentare tathā ||  
  
bhūtapīṭhasya pārśve tu indraṃ saṃpūjayet tathā |  
āgneyādīśaparyantaṃ svasvasthāne vicakṣaṇaḥ || 16 ||  
  
dvārasya uttare pārśve brahmāṇantu prakīrtitam |  
pitāmaheśayormadhye ādityadvādaśantathā ||  
  
bhāskara kṣetrapālañca śāṅkaro vā viśeṣataḥ |  
cakrapāvakayormadhye aśvinyādau tu vinyaset ||  
  
p. 84)  
  
āgneyyayamayormadhye saṃsthāpya saptaro * * |  
yāmye nai-ṛtayormadhye pitṛsthānaṃ vidhīyate ||  
  
nai-ṛtiṃ varuṇayormadhye apsaro gaṇameva ca |  
varuṇavāyuvayormadhye munīnāṃ sthānameva ca ||   
  
vāyavya somayormadhye ityaṣṭau vasavastathā |  
somamīśānayormadhye rudramekādaśaṃ bahi || 17 ||  
  
prathame vā'pi pīṭhe vā ityaṣṭike vā prapūjayet |  
balipīṭhantataḥ kṛtvā caturdikṣu viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
bāhyābhyantarayo pīṭhe pūrvadvāre tu vinyaset |  
antarassarvadevānāṃ piśācā bāhyapīṭhake ||  
  
yakṣāṇāndakṣiṇe caivā rākṣasānāntu paścime |  
gandharvāṇāntu saumyaśca bhūtānāṃ bhūtameva ca ||  
  
tadūrdhve padamityuktaṃ aṣṭaśakti dalannyaset |  
sarvadevamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ agrapīṭhaṃ prakalpayet || 18 ||  
  
tataḥ purasthitaṃ pīṭhaṃ balindadyādviśeṣataḥ |  
  
|| balipīṭhadhyānam ||  
  
mukhapañca samavaktra samanāsinayane |  
daśakarṇadaśabāhu daśaśūladaśadhṛk ||  
  
p. 85)  
  
dalameka hṛdayaṃ atiraktavarṇaṃ dvayapādamiti bhūtabalipīṭha balibhṛk   
  
|| balidhyānam ||  
  
pañcānanaṃ daśabhujaṃ atiraktadehaṃ pāśāṅkuśābhayakaroddhṛta   
kheṭakañca śūlāsibāṇañca dhanuñcacakraṃ vandemahaṃ varatanuṃ   
śivamevarudram ||  
  
|| adhidevatai ||  
  
āmodaśca pramodaśca pramukho durmukhastathā |  
avighno vighnakartā ca pakṣeśi pañcahastathā ||  
  
dvāramantargataṃ vidyāt dvārapālān bahirmukhān |  
balipīṭhaṃ vṛṣaṃ śūlaṃ devasyābhimukhaṃ bhavet || 21 ||  
  
āmodaśyāmavarṇantu pramodaṃ kṛṣṇameva cā |  
pramukhaṃ sphaṭikābhāsaṃ durmukhaṃ kuṅkumaprabham ||  
  
avighno vidrumābhāsaṃ vighnakartāñjanaprabham |  
ityevaṃ varṇabhedantu ṣaḍaite bhūtanāyakāḥ || 22 ||  
  
dvibhujañca dvinetrañca ṭaṅkapāśadharantathā |  
ugradaṃṣṭra samāyuktaṃ bhīmarūpaṃ mahābalam ||  
  
sarvābharaṇa saṃyuktaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam |  
prāsādābhimukhaṃ sarvaṃ dīrghadaṃṣṭrodghaṭānanam || 23 ||  
  
pūrve ca dakṣiṇe caiva uttare paścime tathā |  
  
p. 86)  
  
garbhagṛhasya pañcā ca catuṣkaṃ coktamunnatam |  
tribhāgaṃ madhyamaṃ proktaṃ dvibhāgamadhamaṃ bhavet || 24 ||  
  
dvārotsedhasamaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tattripādantu madhyamam |  
dvārārthamadhamaṃ siddhi vistarotsedha tatsamam ||  
  
vistārasya tribhāgasya hāṭaketaka viṃśati |  
tribhāgenopamekena caturbhirjagatastathā || 25 ||  
  
kampaṃ kṛtvādake dūrdhve tadūrdhve koṭipaṭṭikā |  
karṇaṃ kuryāccaturbhāgerekenaivodyapaṭṭikā ||  
  
mahāpaṭṭikayādūrdhvaṃ senadvaṃśāptalonnatam |  
karṇikāmekabhāgreṇa proktamutsedhamuttam ||  
  
balipīṭhamitikhyātaṃ ṛṣiliṅgaprakīrtitam |  
sarveṣāṃ liṅgamevantu baliṃ tṛptāyate smṛtam || 26 ||  
  
|| bāṇaliṅgabali ||  
  
dharodhruvaśca semaścāpaścaivānilastathā |  
pratyūṣaśca prabhāvaśca vasavo'ṣṭa prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
bāṇaliṅgaṃ tathārogyaṃ balidadyātprakīrtitāḥ |  
tatpūrve dhānyavarṇañca tatpūrvaṃ pūjanakramāt || 27 ||  
  
kramātpūrvabaliṃ kuryāt divyaliṅgamihocyate |  
  
p. 87)  
  
|| rākṣasaliṅgabalidevatai ||  
  
pūrve yakṣagaṇañcaiva rākṣasaṃ gaṇabāṇavat |  
vidhā ca gaṇadakṣiṇyāṅgāṇavaṃ gaṇanai-ṛte ||  
  
kinnarāgaṇavāruṇyāṃ pitṛbhyāṃ gaṇavāyave |  
dānavānāṃ gaṇaṃ saumye aiśānyāṃ gaṇamiśritam || 28 ||  
  
ityeṣāṃ gaṇamevantu balidānantu rākṣasā |  
  
|| pañcaprākāradvāradevatai ||  
  
nityannāmavasānantu prathamadvārapūjayet |  
nandiñcaiva mahākālaṃ dvitīyadvārapūjayet ||   
  
daṇḍinañcaiva muṇḍīnāṃ tritīyadvārapūjayet |  
āmodaśca pramodaśca caturthadvāra pūjayet ||  
  
gaṇeśa skandamevantu pañcaprakārakalpayet |  
dvāradeśe samākhyātaṃ balintatra prakalpayet || 29 ||  
  
|| aṣṭabalidevatai ||  
  
vṛṣāgnimātravighnañca skandajyeṣṭhantathaiva ca |  
durgābhāskara evātha balibhuk aṣṭadevatāḥ || 30 ||  
  
|| balipramāṇam ||  
  
taṇḍulaṃ prasthapādantu baliñcaiva pramāṇakam || 31 ||  
  
p. 88)  
  
nityanaimittikañcaiva baliṃ kṛtvā viśeṣataḥ |  
trisandhyāyāṃ baliṃ kṛtvā anyakāle na kārayet || 32 ||  
  
athā'nyena prakāreṇa kāmyārthañca balindadet |  
mahāhavanivedyante balindadyādviśeṣataḥ || 33 ||  
  
naimittikopasandhyāstu havisānna balindadet |  
nārikela pramāṇantat uttamasya vidhīyate ||  
  
kapitthasya pramāṇantu balindadyāttu madhyamam |  
kukkuṭāṇḍapramāṇañca adhamaṃ balidānakam ||  
  
astamuṣṭipramāṇañca astadvayapramāṇakam |  
śaktimātrapramāṇañca baliṃ sarvasudāpayet || 34 ||  
  
uttamaṃ kabalaṃ proktaṃ madhyamaṃ muṣṭireva ca |  
adhamaṃ āhutiṃ proktaṃ balindadyātprakīrtitaḥ || 35 ||  
  
|| devibalipīṭhadevatai ||  
  
ambikā bhramarādurgā cāmuṇḍā kālarātrayā |  
kaumārikālikādevi vanadurgābaliṃ haret || 36 ||  
  
mahādevi prasādāyāṃ sarve gṛhṇantu śaṅkari |  
  
|| devibalipīṭhādhidevatai ||  
  
ākāśamātaraṃ pūrve dakṣiṇe bhūtamātaram |  
  
p. 89)  
  
vāruṇye astamātarapañcaiva uttare devamātaram |  
anuktamātara śraddhe dadyāt pīṭhāgrake bali || 37 ||  
  
bāṇarāvaṇacanḍeśa nandibhṛṅgi vṛṣādayaḥ |  
sadāśiva prasātoyaṃ sarvaṃ gṛhṇantu śaivakāḥ || 38 ||  
  
|| dhvajadaṇḍadhyānam ||  
  
pīṭhasya devaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ śivākhyaṃ ghaṇṭānanaṃ viṣṇumayañca daṇḍam |  
mālāśca devī caturānanāśca svavarṇamaṇḍadhvaja daṇḍarūpam || 39 ||  
  
ekasya pādaṃ dvimukhaṃ ṣaḍakṣaṃ homāvalīdarbhakarajjumālā |  
śvetāṅga rūpaṃ dvibhujandvināsi ārūḍhapadmāsana daṇḍarūpam || 40 ||  
  
pīṭhaṃ pṛthividaivatyaṃ lokapālādi daivatā |  
bhikṣudaṇḍa upandaṇḍavedi aṣṭarajju maṇidarbhamālikā |  
aṣṭamūrti adhidevamāśraye arcanādi avarohaṇāntakam || 41 ||  
  
pūrve brahmāṇamabhyarcya dakṣiṇe viṣṇumeva ca |  
anantamuttare caiva paścime śaṅkarantathā || 42 ||  
  
ityevaṃ dhvajamūrte tu arcanasya vidhīyate |  
indramagniyamañcaiva ni-ṛ-ṛtiṃ varuṇantathā || 43 ||  
  
vāyusomastathaiśānye pīṭhadik devatā nyaset |  
pūrvena rudramabhyarcya anantaṃ dakṣiṇena tu ||  
  
p. 90)  
  
nāgāya paścime caiva uttare śaṅkarantathā |  
nakṣatrāgneyakañcaiva nir-ṛtiṃ grahapālakam ||  
  
vāyavye'surañcaivā aiśānye dakṣakantathā |  
madhye brahmāṇamabhyarcya daṇḍādyai devatānyaset || 44 ||  
  
|| dhvajapaṭadevatai ||  
  
vṛṣabhaṃ valayachatraṃ cāmaraṃ svastiśūlaṃ  
śaśivasugaṇapādaṃ rudraśaktiñca manye |  
ṛṣabha dhavalapaṭṭaṃ darpaṇaṃ pūrṇakumbhaṃ  
dhvajapaṭa iti devaṃ dīpaśaṅkhañca pālye || 45 ||  
  
pīṭhantu pārvatīndevaṃ daṇḍasya rudradevatam |  
iṣṭi skanda samāyuktaṃ upadaṇḍavināyakam ||  
  
mālā brahmasamāyuktaṃ pādañcaivāyudaivatam |  
vāsukī rajjudaivatyaṃ vṛṣabhantu janārdanam ||  
  
cāmarau candrasūryau ca chatraṃ sarasvatī bhavet |  
dīpantu śrī mahālakṣmi ghaṇṭānādaṃ ṣaḍānanam || 46 ||  
  
ityevaṃ devatābhyarcya dhvajadaṇḍaprakīrtitāḥ |  
  
|| navagrahadhyānam ||  
  
ādityamekavaktrañca dvinetraṃ raktavarṇakam |  
  
p. 91)  
  
raktāmbaradharañcaiva raktaśchatra dhvajānvitam |  
raktavarṇadharañcaiva saptāśvaṃ raktameva ca ||  
  
saptarajju sa raktañca dvibhujaṃ raktamadmajam |  
parimaṇḍala madhyasthaṃ raktapadmāsana sthitam ||  
  
pūrvābhimukhamevantu giriṇāñca pradakṣiṇam |  
kaliṅgadeśe rājñāñca kāśyapagotrameva ca || 47 ||  
  
viśākhanirkṣejātañca raviṃ dhyātvā namāmyaham |  
ekavaktraṃ dvisomañca dvinetraṃ śvetavarṇakam ||  
  
śvetāmbaradharañcaiva śvetavarṇarathaṃ tathā |  
śvetacchatra dhvajañcaiva daśāśvaṃ śvetavarṇakam ||  
  
śvetavarṇarajorajjuṃ dvibhujaṃ kumudantathā |  
catuṣkoṇa sumadhyena śvetapadmāsanasthitam ||  
  
paścimābhi mukhañcaiva girīṇāñca pradakṣiṇam |  
āgneyadiśimevantu varāṭe daśarājyakam ||  
  
ātreya gotramevantu kṛttikā-ṛkṣajātañca |  
lokarakṣāyate caiva dhyātvā somaṃ namāmyaham |  
  
raktavarṇadvinetrañca ekavaktrañcaturbhujam || 48 ||  
  
raktāmbara dharañcaiva raktapuṣparathaṃ tathā |  
  
p. 92)  
  
raktaśchatra dhvajañcaiva śaktiśūlagadādharam |  
trikoṇākāra madhyasthaṃ dakṣiṇābhimukhantathā ||  
  
giripradakṣiṇañcaiva dakṣiṇe diśasaṃsthitam |  
vijayadaśādhi pañcaiva bhāradvājena gotrajam || 49 ||  
  
aśvinī-ṛkṣajātañca aṅgārakanamāmyaham |  
ekavaktrandvinetrañca pītavarṇabudhantathā ||  
  
pītavarṇarathañcaiva pītaśchatra suśobhitam |  
pītāmbaradharañcaiva dhanurbāṇantathaiva ca ||  
  
bāṇākārasya madhyena vīrasiṃhāsana sthitam |  
pūrvābhimukhamevantu īśānadiśi saṃsthitam ||  
  
magadhādhipatiñcaiva girīṇāñca pradakṣiṇam |  
ātreyagotramevantu śravaṇena tu janmakam || 50 ||  
  
ityeva rūpamevantu budhaṃ dhyātvā namāmyaham |  
dvinetraṃ pītavarṇañca ekavaktrañcaturbhujam ||  
  
pītāmbaradharañcaiva pītavarṇarathādhipam |  
pītaśchatra dhvajañcaiva catuśśṛṅgasya madhyagam ||  
  
yogāsanasamañcaiva uttarābhimukhantathā |  
abhayaṃ varadañcaivākṣasūtrakamaṇḍalum ||  
  
p. 93)  
  
uttareṇa diśiñcaiva giriṇāñca pradakṣiṇam |  
sindhūradeśe rājñāñca gotramāṅgīrasantathā ||  
  
jātamuttara phalgunyāṃ devasya gurumeva ca |  
ityevaṃ rūpamevantu bṛhaspatinnamāmyaham || 51 ||  
  
śvetavarṇantu śukreṇa ekavaktraṃ dvihastakam |  
śvetavastreṇa saṃyuktaṃ ekanetrārakāyutam ||  
  
śvetacchatra dhvajañcaiva śvetavarṇarathādhipam |  
pañcakoṇasyamadhyena citrasiṃhāsana sthitam ||  
  
pūrvābhimukhamevantu gadāvaradahastakam |  
guṇadeśādhi patiñcaiva girīṇāñca pradakṣiṇam ||  
  
gotraṃ bhārgavamevantu jyeṣṭhānakṣatra jātakam |  
pūrvadik sthitamevantu rākṣasān gurudeva ca || 52 ||  
  
ityevaṃ rūpamevantu bhagavān śukraṃ namāmyaham |  
ekavaktrandvinetrañca dvibhujaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇakam ||  
  
kṛṣṇāmbaradharañcaiva kṛṣṇaśchatra dhvajantathā |  
kṛṣṇavarṇarathañcaiva dhanurākāramaṇḍalam ||  
  
kṛṣṇasiṃhāsanañcaiva madhye pratyaṅmukhasthitam |  
śūlaṃ dhanurdharañcaiva paścime diśi saṃsthitam ||  
  
p. 94)  
  
āndhradeśādhipañcaivā girīṇāñca pradakṣiṇim |  
kāśyapa gotramevantu revatī jananantathā || 53 ||  
  
grajavāhanamevantu śaniṃ dhyātvā namāmyaham |  
dvinetraṃ nīlavarṇañca trihastamekavaktrakam ||  
  
nīlāmbaradharañcaiva nīlavarṇarathādhipam |  
nīlaśchatra dhvajañcaiva kṛṣṇaśūrpasya maṇḍalam ||  
  
nīlasiṃhāsanaṃ madhye dakṣiṇābhimukhantathā |  
pūrvadeśādhi pañcaiva khaḍgacarmatriśūlakam ||  
  
giripradakṣiṇañcaiva jāmunīgotrameva ca |  
bharaṇījananañcaivā rāhuṃ dhyātvā namāmyaham || 54 ||  
  
citravarṇadvinetrañca dvihastaṃ ekavaktrakam |  
citrāmbaradharañcaiva dhvajarathaṃ tathā ||  
  
maṇḍale tu dhvajākāraṃ madhye citrāsanantathā |  
vanadeśādhipañcaiva vāyavyāndiśi saṃsthitam ||  
  
jaimunigotramevantu āśleṣā jananantathā |  
vikṛtān bhagavāṃścaiva girīṇāñca pradakṣiṇam || 55 ||  
  
ityetadvarṇamevantu dhyātvā ketuṃ namāmyaham |  
  
|| astradevadhyānam ||  
  
p. 95)  
  
triṇetraṃ raktavarṇañca ūrdhvakeśaṃ sudaṃṣṭrakam |  
kapālaṃ śūlakaṃ padmaṃ kamaṇḍalvakṣadhāriṇam ||  
  
ūruhastadvipādañca kiñcidbrahmasitānanam |  
koṭikoṭyā mahājjvālaṃ udyatkoṭi raviprabham ||  
  
astradeva śivājjvālaṃ brahmāviṣṇusvarūpiṇam |  
astradevaṃ sadādhyātvā pratiṣṭhotsava karmaṇi || 56 ||  
  
astraśastrapraśamanaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam |  
  
asuraharasurāstraṃ śūlamāmaṇḍalāgraṃ  
sakalasuramayāntaṃ śambhuhastaṃ priyaṃ syāt |  
triśikhasahitavahniṃ vāyurākāśa mūrtiṃ  
jvalanapatitakāntiṃ astradeva svarūpam || 57 ||  
  
triśūlaṃ vṛṣabhāgre tu astramūrtiṃ caturbhujam |  
kūrparaṃ śṛṅgamadhye tu ūrumadhyantu vāmake ||  
  
mṛgaṭaṅkaṃ samāyuktaṃ vyāghracarmaṇavāsasam |  
sarvatīrtheṣu sānnidhyaṃ dhyātvā mantreṇa pūjayet || 58 ||  
  
vibhūti  
  
triṇetraṃ triśiraṃ raudraṃ triguṇaṃ raktavastrakam |  
tripādaṃ vahninayanaṃ bhasmakuṇḍitavigraham || 59 ||  
  
p. 96)  
  
śāntaṃ rūpa sukhāsīnaṃ bhasmarūpamiti smṛtam |  
  
śokkapānai  
  
ekasya pādaṃ daśacāṣṭahastaṃ daśāṣṭaśūlaṃ śirapañca trinetram |  
unmīlavaktraṃ daśakarṇayuktaṃ uddīptakeśaṃ atidīpta hutāśana liṅgam ||  
  
abhayaṃ varadaṃ śāntaṃ kāntālanta vivigraham |  
mṛgat śūkakaro taṃ vadanāmaṇibhūṣaṇam ||  
  
naṭilanayanaṃ ḍiṇḍimuktendrāmaṇi bhūṣaṇam |  
nigamana garinādaṃ vande kundendusitaram || 61 ||  
  
|| ṣaḍādhāradalam ||  
  
ādhārantu caturdalaṃ ruṇarasan vāsāntavarṇāśriyaṃ   
svādhiṣṭhānamanekavaidyutanibhaṃ bālānna ṣaṭvatrikam |  
raktābhaṃ maṇipūrakaṃ daśadalaṃ mādyaṃ vikārābdhakaṃ  
patraiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ svanāhatadahai mama rimānnāvratam ||  
  
mātrābhidvidiśaṣoḍaśasvarayutaṃ jyotirviśuddhāmbujaṃ   
halaityakṣarabījayugmasayutaṃ raktābhamājñāmbujam |  
tasmādūrdhvagataṃ prabhadisitaṃ padmaṃ sahasraśchadaṃ   
nityānandamayaṃ sadāśivapadaṃ nityānnamasyodaram || 62 ||  
  
mūlādhārasvādhiṣṭhāna maṇipūrakahanāhata viśuddhākhyai-  
  
p. 97)  
  
ājñāyamidha ī mūlādhāra vighneśa dhyānam ||  
  
gajavaktrañca raktābhaṃ triṇetrañca mahodaram |  
dantapāśāṅkuśāpūpaṃ cārubāhu catuṣṭayam ||  
  
mahādeva sutaṃ mūlaṃ mantramūrtimahaṃ bhaje || 63 ||  
  
|| svādhiṣṭhānaṃ brahmām ||  
  
hemākāraṃ caturvaktraṃ śubhravastropavītinam |  
sṛgakṣamālākalaśaṃ daṇḍacārucaturbhujam || 64 ||  
  
netrāṣṭaka samāyuktaṃ nityaṃ vande pitāmaham |  
  
|| maṇipūrakaṃ viṣṇu ||  
  
lakṣmīkāntañca nīlābhaṃ śaṅkhañca mṛgagadādharam |  
śrīvatsalāñcanaṃ devaṃ pītāmbara virājitam ||  
  
vanamālākirīṭañca kuṇḍale dadhatassadā |  
abhayaṃ sarvadevānāṃ ambujākṣamanāmayam || 65 ||  
  
anekāditya saṃkāśaṃ vande viṣṇumaninditam |  
  
|| anāhate rudrar ||  
  
kṣīrābhaṃ kālakaṇṭhañca tritreṃ candraśeram |  
gaṅgādharañcaturbāhuṃ triśūlāgni varadābhayam ||  
  
jñānamudradharandevaṃ gaṅgendrakṛta kiṅkiṇām |  
  
p. 98)  
  
puṇḍarīkāñjanadharaṃ bhūtiśobhita vigraham |  
pralayodarakartāraṃ vanderudraṃ pinākinam || 66 ||  
  
|| viśuddhākhye maheśvarar ||  
  
ṭaṅkhakundenduśobhāḍhyaṃ śārdūlājinavāsinam |  
indugaṅgā jaṭācūṭaṃ maheśākhyaṃ mahedyutim ||  
  
arkendu vahninayanaṃ kālakaṇṭhamanāmayam |  
caṇḍāṃśukoṭisadṛśaṃ sarpayajñopavītinam ||  
  
varadābhayapāśāḍhyaṃ vāmadakṣiṇabāhukam |  
paraśuṃ ḍamaruñcāpi dadhānañcātmarūpiṇam || 67 ||  
  
vāme maheśvarī yuktaṃ vande devamaheśvaram |  
  
|| ājñeya sadāśivam ||  
  
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ dvātriṃśallakṣaṇānvitam |  
vṛktapadmāsinaṃ pañca * * vaktaṃ manoharam ||  
  
tripañcanayanañcāsyaṃ somacūḍaśubhāvaham |  
daśabāhasamāyuktaṃ citrakāyajināmbaram ||  
  
varadābhayasaṃyuktaṃ vāmadakṣiṇahastakam |  
śūlavajrātathā khaḍgaṃ paraśuṃ pāśameva ca ||  
  
nāgaṃ vahniñca dadhataṃ śāntarūpiṇam |  
  
p. 99)  
  
pañcāvaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ pañcakṛtya parāyaṇam |  
pañcākṣarajapaṃ devaṃ pañcamantra mahātanum ||  
  
aṣṭatriṃśatkalopetaṃ ādi madhyāntavarjitam |  
vidyānāmārthi bhakteśaṃ bindunādasamanvitam ||  
  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśatattvanāyakam |  
manonmati samāyuktaṃ vande devaṃ sadāśivam || 68 ||  
  
|| saccidānantam ||  
  
ṣaḍādhārāpare mūrdhnīṃ sahasradalapaṅkaje |  
gurunāthaṃ kṛpāmūrtiṃ japākusumasannibham ||  
  
dvinetraṃ dvibhujaṃ śāntaṃ raktavastrānulepanam |  
raktotpaladharaṃ nityaṃ māṇikyamakuṭojjvalam ||  
  
tattvādhikaparaṃ śaktiṃ sākṣāmūrti pradāyakam |  
sanmārgadeśikaṃ vande saccidānandavigraham || 69 ||  
  
|| nandidhyānam ||  
  
triṇetrañcaturbhujañcaivābhayaṃ varadānvitam |  
ugratomaraśūlañcākṣamālā samanvitam || 70 ||  
  
raktavastrasamāyuktaṃ nandinaṃ saṃprapūjayet |  
  
|| nandikeśvaradhyānam ||  
  
p. 100)  
  
raktaṃ triṇetraṃ jaṭilaṃ savyavāmakaradvayam |  
akṣamālātriśūlañca dadhānaṃ nandikeśvaram || 71 ||  
  
|| nandiśakti ||  
  
makarāsanagāṅgaṃ * * * * * * * piṇīm |  
dvinetraṃ dvibhujañcaiva meropari saṃsthitam |  
dakṣanīlotpalañcaiva pūrṇakumbhantu vāmake || 72 ||  
  
śuklavastreṇa saṃyuktaṃ citravastreṇa bhūṣitām |  
nandiñca dakṣiṇe bhāge dhyātvā gaṅgāṃ prapūjayet || 73 ||  
  
|| nandikeśvara anujñai ||  
  
nandikeśa māhābhāgā sarvābhīṣṭaphalapradā |  
śaṅkareṇa tu pūjāyāṃ anujñāndā tu marhasi || 74 ||  
  
|| nandiśaktyānujñai ||  
  
mahānandī ca gaṅgāyāṃ sarvaloka prayāvahi |  
nandikeśasya vāmeṇa śuklavarṇasvarūpiṇī || 75 ||  
  
mahādevi ca pūjāyāṃ anujñāndātu marhasi |  
  
|| mahākālar ||  
  
kṛṣṇatryakṣaṃ mahākālaṃ vāmasavyakāradvaye |  
kapālañca triśūlañca dadhānaṃ vikaṭānanam || 76 ||  
  
p. 101)  
  
caturbhujantriṇetrañca kapālaṃ śūlameva cā |  
dakṣiṇe bhayamevañca vāme pāśasamanvitam ||  
  
jaṭāmakuṭasaṃyuktaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam |  
kṛṣṇavarṇamiti proktaṃ mahākālasvarūpakam || 77 ||  
  
|| śakti ||  
  
śyāmāṅkūrma sthitāṃ * * yamunāñca vibhāvayet |  
śyāmavarṇañcaturhastaṃ savyahaste ghaṭantathā ||  
  
dakṣahastena rājanīṃ savye nīlotpalantathā |  
nīmbasya phalamevantu dakṣahastena vinyaset || 78 ||  
  
sarvālaṅkāra saṃyuktaṃ yamunāyai prapūjayet |  
mahākāla mahāteja sarvalokaprayāvahā || 79 ||  
  
śaṅkareṇa pūjāyāṃ anujñāṃ dātumarhasi |  
  
|| śaktyanujñai ||  
  
sāgaro yamunāyai ca śyāmavarṇa śarīriṇi |  
mahākālasya vāmena sarvalokaika rakṣaṇi || 80 ||   
  
śaṅkarīṇa tu pūjāyāṃ anujñāndātumarhasi |  
  
|| bhairavānujñai ||  
  
ekavaktraṃ śirojjvālāṃ raktanetraṃ caturbhujam |  
  
p. 102)  
  
dvipādaṃ śvānavāhañca khaṇḍakhaḍga sakhaiṭakam |  
digambaraṃ triśūlañca devatālaya rakṣaṇaḥ || 81 ||  
  
deva pūjāyateścaiva udghaṭī tamanujñayā |  
  
|| kuccikkol ||  
  
udghāṭirūpamevantu trikoṇasya vidhīyate |  
valayañca tataḥ kṛtvā varṇaṃ rajitameva ca || 82 ||  
  
devadvārakavāṭaiśca bandhanādityarūpakam |  
adhasya pṛthivi daivatyaṃ daṇḍaṃ kārkoṭakaṃ tathā ||  
  
valayaṃ brahmadaivatyaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇustathaiva ca |  
agre rudrādhidaivatyaṃ udghāṭisyādhi devatā || 83 ||  
  
valayaṃ durgamevantu daṇḍañcaiva suvīryakā |  
madhyakoṇeṣu kālīñca agrakoṇādhi bhairavam || 83 ||  
  
devārcanādiyuktañca dvikālasya prapūjayet |  
devadvāre ca dakṣiṇyāṃ vijayaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇakam ||  
  
sthambākāran dvinetrañca dvipādañca dvihastakam |  
khaḍgakheṭa samāyuktaṃ svarṇābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
devadvārañca kartā ca vijayañca vidhīrbhavet || 84 ||  
  
|| vaḍakkunilai ||  
  
p. 103)  
  
dvārasyottara pārśve tu vijayañca nīlavarṇakam |  
svarṇamābharaṇairyuktaṃ ekavaktraṃ dvipādakam ||  
  
dvihastañca dvinetrañca triśūlaṃ paraśuntathā |  
stambhākārasya vijñeyaṃ vijayañca vidhirbhavet || 85 ||  
  
|| melpaṭṭi ||  
  
padaṅga śyāmavarṇañca ekavaktrañcaturbhujam |  
khaḍgakheṭa samāyuktaṃ kapālaṃ śaktimeva ca ||  
  
rudrākṣamupavītañca śvetavastra sudhāraṇam |  
pataṅgāya svarūpantu arcanāyavidhirbhavet || 86 ||  
  
|| kīṣaṃpaṭṭi ||  
  
bhuvaṅga śyāmavarṇañcābhūṣaṇannīlaratnakam |  
pītāmbaropavītañca ekavaktrañcaturbhujam ||  
  
triśūlaṃ ḍamaruñcaiva daṇḍapāśantathaiva ca |  
bhuvaṅgāyasvarūpantu arcanādi vidhirbhavet || 87 ||  
  
|| kavāṭarandhram ||  
  
suṣirāntargate candraḥ suṣiraḥ parasūryayoḥ |  
tanmadhye vāyusañcāraṃ tridevaṃ suṣirasthitam || 88 ||  
  
|| tāppāl ||  
  
p. 104)  
  
ghaṭṭaṃ dakṣiṇapārśve tu vighaṭṭamuttare tathā |  
kavāṭe pūrvabhāgena bandhanādikramantathā || 89 ||  
  
devapūjāmanujñāya kavāṭo ghāṭanaṃ bhavet |  
  
|| kavāṭaṃ poḍuhuradu ||  
  
sakarṇasya tu raktañca vimalaṃ pṛṣṭhapārśvayoḥ |  
pañcakoṇa svarūpañca ekahastasamanvitam || 90 ||  
  
devadvārādi nṛttañca devapūjāmanujñayā |  
  
|| adhidevatai ||  
  
sadāśivaśiraḥ koṇe karṇakoṇeṣu rudrakam |  
hṛdaye viṣṇurūpantu kaṭikoṇe caturmukham ||  
  
pādakoṇeṣuvīrañca vikarṇasyādhidevatā |  
  
|| vaḍakoṭikku ||  
  
sukarṇaṃ nīlarūpañca suvāhapṛṣṭha pārśvayoḥ |  
pañcakoṇamiti proktaṃ ekahastasamanvitam || 91 ||  
  
devapūjāmanujñāyāṃ devadvāreṇa rakṣaṇa |  
  
|| adhidevatai ||  
  
agrakoṇe manonmanyāṃ karṇakoṇeṣu śaṅkari |  
lakṣmī ca hṛdayañcaiva kaṭikoṇe sarasvati || 92 ||  
  
p. 105)  
  
pādakoṇeṣukāliñca vikarṇasyādhi devatā |  
  
|| dakṣiṇakavāṭam ||  
  
vimalaṃ pūruṣākāraṃ * * * ñca caturbhujam |  
śūlañca hariṇañcaiva pāśamaṅkurameva ca ||  
  
ūrdhvaśikhāya saṃyuktaṃ pādamekantathaiva ca |  
svarṇamābharaṇañcaiva vimalasya prakīrtitāḥ || 93 ||  
  
|| uttarakavāṭe ||  
  
subāhuṃ pūruṣaṃ divyaṃ svarṇavarṇasudhāriṇam |  
śikhā ūrdhvasamañcaiva ekavaktraṃ caturbhujam ||  
  
ṭaṅkaśūladharañcaiva daṇḍapadmatathaiva ca |  
rudrākṣamupavītañca ekapādena vinyaset || 94 ||  
  
|| kavāṭānujñai ||  
  
subāhuṃ vimalañcaiva devadvāre ca rakṣaṇā |  
devakāryādhikartā ca devapūjāmanujñayā || 95 ||  
  
|| kadavutarakka ||  
  
pañcākṣasī pāṭahiraṇyavāsi pampāpurīnātha parāpareśa |  
viśveśvaraṃ viśvamantamūrti kavāṭamudghāṭanakālanālam || 96 ||  
  
|| kadavuśātta ||  
  
p. 106)  
  
sarvāntarāyāmi vabhovaśambho rakṣājagatkāraṇaviśvamūrte |  
prasādamantargatabhāvaśrutyāṃ kavāṭabandhāvidhehanujñā || 97 ||  
  
digambarāya śūrāya divyatejassvarūpiṇe |  
ṛṣipatni vimohāya devattalaya rakṣaṇā ||  
  
devapūjāñca kāle ca kavāṭo bandhanasya ca |  
ughaṭīta samañcaiva gṛhītvā gaṇasevitam || 98 ||  
  
|| caṇḍeśvarar ||  
  
śrī kundalīmakuṭa dṛgvayasaumyavaktraṃ karṇadvayemakarakuṇḍala   
yajñasūtraḥ astāñjali vijayasairya sabāhuṭaṅkaṃ caṇḍeśvara pādāmbuja   
mānatomyaham |  
  
punaḥ-  
  
dvinetraṃ dvibhujaṃ śyāmaṃ ṭaṅkañcaiva tu dhāriṇam |  
dvipādāñjali hastañca sarvābharaṇa bhūṣitam || 100 ||  
  
jaṭāmakuṭasaṃyuktaṃ caṇḍarūpamiti smṛtam |  
caṇḍeśvarañcaturbāhuṃ caturvaktrantrilocanam ||  
  
bibhratkamaṇḍaluṃ śūlaṃ akṣasūtraṃ paraśvadham |  
mahoragopavītāḍhyastannivartita kaṅkaṇaḥ || 101 ||  
  
dhyeye navāmbudābhāsaṃ samayādi niyāmakaḥ |  
  
|| dhvaniścaṇḍeśvarar ||  
  
rudrāgne prabhavaṃ caṇḍaṃ kajjalābhaṃ bhayānakam |  
  
p. 107)  
  
śūlaṭaṅkadharaṃ rudraṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbhujam |  
mukhotkīrṇa mahājjvālaṃ raktaṃ dvādaśalocanam ||  
  
jaṭāmakuṭakhaṇḍendu maṇḍitaṃ phaṇikaṅkaṇam |  
vyālayajñopavītañca akṣasūtraṃ kamaṇḍalum ||  
  
dantapadmāsanāsīnaṃ bhaktiḥ prahvārtināśanam |  
caṇḍeśvara vimānasthaṃ syakarmāṇa kṛtinnamaḥ ||  
  
īśvarāśāpatiṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gaṇeśāvaraṇe sthitam || 102 ||  
  
|| caṇḍaśakti ||  
  
dvinetraṃ dvibhujāḥ śyāmāmakṣamālāntu kuṇḍikām |  
stanau bandhasamāyuktaṃ jaṭāmakuṭadhāriṇīm ||  
  
tathaiva śaṅkarīṃ dhyātvā caṇḍaśakti vidhīrbhavet || 103 ||  
  
|| hanumantadhyānam ||  
  
amalakanakavarṇaṃ prajjvalaṃ pāvakākṣaṃ  
sarasijanibhavaktraṃ sarvadā suprasannam |  
padutarakhanagātraṃ kuṇḍalālaṅkṛtāsyaṃ  
raṇajayakarapālaṃ rāmadūtannamāmi || 104 ||  
  
dhyāyedbāladivākaraṃ dṛtinibhaṃ devāri darbhāpahaṃ  
deveda pramukha praśasiti yaśasīṃ te divyamāniṃ rucim |  
  
p. 108)  
  
sugrīvādi samastavānarayutaṃ savyakta tattvapriyaṃ  
saṃratnāruṇa locanaṃ pavanajaṃ pītāmbarālaṅkṛtam ||  
vande vidyudvalayavilasat brahmasūtre pariṣṭhaṃ  
karṇadvandve kanakavalayaṃ maṇḍalollāsavaktram |  
raktaścihne kanakaravajite kuṇḍale dhārayantaṃ  
satkaupīnaṃ kapivarahitaṃ kāmarūpaṃ kavīndram || 105 ||  
  
vaidehī ghanaśokatāpaharaṇo vaikuṇṭhabhaktapriyam |  
akṣyādurjatarākṣaseśvara mahādarpāpahārīraṇe  
so'haṃ * * * sadā cāsmān samīrātmajam || 106 ||  
  
|| garuḍan ||  
  
ajānutaṃ suvarṇābhaṃ akaṭyastu samaprabham |  
kuṅkumāruṇamākarṇaṃ raktākṣaṃ nāgabhūṣaṇam ||  
  
piṅgalākṣaṃ garutmantaṃ suvarṇasadṛśa prabham |  
dīrghabāhuṃ bṛhaskandaṃ nāgābharaṇabhūṣitam ||  
  
anantavāsukaṭake yajñasūtrantu vāsukīm |  
takṣakārkoṭa sūtrantu harakārkoṭakastathā ||  
  
padmadakṣiṇakarṇe tu mahāpdamassunāmatā |  
  
p. 109)  
  
śaṅkhaśśirapradeśe tu gulikastu bhujāntare |  
evandhyātvā trisandhyāyāṃ ātmānaṃ garuḍarūpiṇam || 107 ||  
  
|| aṣṭamaṅgalam ||  
  
darpaṇaṃ pūrṇakumbhañca vṛṣabhaṃ yugmacāmaram |  
śrīvatsaṃ svastikaṃ śaṅkhaṃ dīpo devāṣṭamaṅgalam || 108 ||  
  
|| aṣṭamaṅgalaśakti ||  
  
umādevi dharādevi kāverī jāhnavī tathā |  
śriyaṃ devī sarasvatyāṃ śaśirdevī ca dīpakām |  
eteṣu cāsaraproktāṃ aṣṭamaṅgalaśaktayaḥ || 109 ||  
  
|| daśāyudhaśakti ||  
  
vilāsinī virūpī cā dhāriṇī sundarī tathā |  
nirmalī durmukhī caivamābhṛt haṃsavilāsinīm || 110 ||  
  
ete daśāyudhānāntu śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
|| astradevar ||  
  
pīṭhaṃ padmañca daṇḍaṃ ghaṭaghaṭavadanaṃ pālikāpadmayuktaṃ   
tripatrajyotirūpaṃ sakalasuramayaṃ śūlarūpaṃ śivāstram | madhye rudrañca   
dakṣetara vidhiharitat śaktibhaḥ pālikāyāṃ kumbhaṃ vighnaṃ viśākhaṃ   
vadanaraviyutaṃ daṇḍamūle tu caṇḍam |  
madhyāhnārka samaprabhaṃ śaśidharaṃ bhīmāṭṭahāsojjvalaṃ tryakṣaṃ   
pannagabhūṣaṇaṃ mṛgadharaṃ piṅgojjvalaṃ mūrdhvajam | hastābjaiśikhāṃ   
mudgaramayīṃ ghaṇṭaṃ kapālaṃdha daṃṣṭrātyugramukhākaraṃ paśupate   
divyāstra rūpaṃ bhaje || 112 ||  
  
p. 110)  
  
|| naṭeśvarar ||  
  
abhayaṃ ḍamarukañcaiva bhujaṅgamagnipātrakam |  
sarpakaṅkaṇa saṃyuktaṃ śuklayajñopavītinam ||  
  
kuñcitaṃ ūrdhvapādañca abhasmāroparisthitam |  
prasannavadanaṃ śāntaṃ pādakiṅkiṇiśobhitam ||  
  
bhūtadyādhārasaṃyuktaṃ tritreṃ sphaṭikaprabham |  
gaṅgā indudharaṃ kṛtvā śirapaścāccirantathā ||113 ||  
  
umayā sahitaṃ devaṃ nṛttarājaṃ prapūjayet |  
  
|| somāskandar nāyakara ||  
  
ṭaṅkakṛṣṇakarandevaṃ abhayaṃ varadantathā |  
vāme nidrita pādaṃ syāt dakṣapādāvalambanam ||  
  
ekāsane tu śaktiḥ syāt madhye bālakumārakam |  
candracūḍakirīṭañca somāskande śamīśvaram || 114 ||  
  
|| vṛṣabha vāhanārūḍha dhyānam ||  
  
ṭaṅkameṇakarandevaṃ paśupāśakarambhavet |  
śaktimadhyamapādaṃ syāt vṛṣārūḍhaśivaṃ bhaje || 115 ||  
  
|| śrī balināyakam ||  
  
abhayavaradahastaṃ ṭaṅkameṇaṃ śubhāṅgaṃ  
samapadasamayuktaṃ candracūḍantriṇetram |  
  
p. 111)  
  
himakarakiraṇaṃ syāt baddhaveṇīkirīṭaṃ  
mama bhava bhavanāśaṃ śrī baliṃ bhāvayāmi || 116 ||  
  
|| pallakkuśokkar ||  
  
savye lambitapādaṃ syāt śaktipādañca nidritam |  
ṭaṅkameṇadharandevaṃ abhayaṃ varadantathā ||  
  
umayā sahitaṃ devaṃ cibikeśamahaṃ bhaje || 117 ||  
  
|| kudirai śokkar ||  
  
samapādaṃ keśabhārañca khalināstaṃ śarāstakam |  
suprasannaṃ kṛtvā mūrtiṃ hayavāhanamīśvaram || 118 ||  
  
|| vṛṣabham ||  
  
sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ śṛṅgaṃ syāt karṇamākāśamārutam |  
netrañca candrasūryaṃ syāt śivaśaktiṣu nāsikā ||  
  
sarvadevamukhaṃ kṛtvā pucchaṃ guhyena brahmayoḥ |  
pañcāṅgaṃ gātraromaṃ syāt vṛttamāsanapīṭhakam || 119 ||  
  
|| dhvaniścaṇḍar ||  
  
abhayahastadharaṃ ṭaṅkaṃ varadadvayahastake |  
nidritaṃ lambapādañca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 120 ||  
  
upavītaṃ śivābrahmaṃ kuṇḍaladhvani caṇḍakam |  
  
p. 112)  
|| bhairavar ||  
  
dhvanitaṃ pāśaśūlañca kapālaṃ śvānavāhanam |  
nirvāṇaṃ raudrarūpañca jvālā jaṭilabhairavam ||  
  
sarpayajñopavītañca muṇḍamālāśaśīdharam |  
daṇḍañca daṃṣṭriṇaṃ kṛtvā āpatoddhāra vigraham || 121 ||  
  
|| śāstā ||  
  
śyāmavarṇa śarīrasuyauvanaṃ tuṅga bhṛṅga sahasrakundalam |  
yogaveṣṭika padmasukhāsanaṃ vāmapuṣkala dakṣiṇapūrṇayoḥ || 122 ||  
  
|| māṇikkavāsahar ||  
  
ekavaktrandvinayanaṃ hastadvaṃ puṣpakantathā |  
jñānamudrākarañcaiva bhasmoddhūlita lepanam ||  
  
rudrākṣamālābharaṇaṃ sarvalakṣaṇaśobhitam |  
māṇikkavācakamityuktaṃ dhyātvā devaṃ samarpayet || 123 ||  
  
ekamukha yugmakara savyajapamālā vāmakarapustakavibhūtidharadeham |  
ābharaṇarudrākṣamālādharamaulīṃ vātapurināyaka svarūpamiti vande || 124 ||  
  
p. 113)  
  
|| sundramūrti ||  
  
svarṇāṅgaṃ netrayugmaṃ vadanapulahitaṃ keśabaddhaṃ śikhāgraṃ  
savye hastāgrapārśvaṃ kaṭakasahayutaṃ vāmabhāge prayuktam |  
vidyudbhṛṅgārabhṛṅgaṃ ubhayakaratalaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ karṇapūṣyaṃ   
śṛṅgāraṃ śaiva vipraṃ sakalakalayutaṃ śrīsundareśaṃ namāmi || 125 ||  
  
|| asmar ||  
  
rudrākṣadhāmaśivapāda yutottamāṅgaṃ saumyānanaṃ   
śivasulāñcanakarṇapūṣya hastāñjatriṇahatāyudha dakṣabāhuṃ padmasthitaṃ   
kavi suvārkapatimānatoska || 126 ||  
  
|| sambāndhār ||  
  
śvetābhaṃ maṇikuṇḍalaṃ puraśikhaṃ saumyaprasannānanaṃ  
savye tarjani dīrghayāmavadṛśaṃ vāme payaḥ pātrakam |  
nirvāṇaṃ śivamambujastutipadaṃ bauddhapravidhvaṃsakaṃ  
nānādrāviḍasatkaviṃ śubhakaraṃ jñānassamandhaṃ bhaje || 127 ||  
  
|| bauddhar ||  
  
dvibhujaṃ ekavaktrantu ūruhastadvilāsanam |  
yogapaṭṭadharandevaṃ vande bauddhāvatārakam ||  
  
sarvadeva namastubhyaṃ tripurasaṃhārasādhakam |  
dharmaśāstrantu vyākhyānaṃ parabrahmasvarūpakam || 128 ||  
  
p. 114)  
  
jñānakaivalya mokṣārthaṃ dhyāyedbauddhanamo'stute |  
  
|| dhvajadaṇḍam ||  
  
yaṣṭitriyaṃ triyyavaktraṃ śaraddṛṣṭiñca locanam |  
darbhagātra kṛpādevaṃ caturhastaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
śūlacakra namaskāraṃ pratyaṅmukhasamaṃ padam |  
dhvajadaṇḍamiti dhyānaṃ buddhimān deśikottamaḥ || 129 ||  
  
|| dvārapālaḥ ||  
  
raktavarṇandvinetrañca nāgayajñopavītinam |  
bhīmarūpasamaṃ kṛṣṭhadvibhujañcaikavaktrakam ||  
  
vismayaṃ hastasaṃyuktaṃ daṇḍāyudhasamanvitam |  
sarva sthitā sthitaṃ devaṃ ḍiṇḍiṇāñca svarūpakam || 130 ||  
  
muṇḍināṃ kṛṣṇavarṇantu dvibhujañca dvinetrakam |  
daṇḍāyudha samāyuktaṃ nāgābharaṇabhūṣitam || 131 ||  
  
vasitaṃ hastisaṃyuktaṃ muṇḍināñca svarūpakam |  
  
|| indradhyānam ||  
  
dvibhujā ca dvinetrā ca śyāmavarṇa samāyutam |  
savya hastevahaṃ vajraṃ vāmahaste'bhayantathā ||  
  
raktāmbara samāyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
hastivāhanasaṃyuktaṃ indrasyākṛtirucyate || 132 ||  
  
p. 115)  
  
|| agni ||  
  
dvibhujā ca dvinetrā ca raktavarṇa sthitānanam |  
āsīnañca samāyuktaṃ mūrdhvakeśāya dīpikam ||  
  
pītavastrasamāyuktaṃ sarvapuṣpairalaṅkṛtam |  
śuklayajñopavītañca śuklavastrottarīyakam ||  
  
sruvaṃ vai savyadhāruṇyaṃ sruksruvaṃ vāmakantathā |  
ajavāhanamevoktaṃ vahnirākṛtirucyate || 133 ||  
  
|| yamaḥ ||  
  
kālañcaninibhākāre vidyutsamaśadaṃṣṭrakam |  
dvibhujaṃ raktakeśañca kuñcitaṃ dvitavibhramam ||  
  
daṇḍāyudhasamāyuktaṃ mahiṣasya tu vāhanam |  
dvinetrañca dvipādañca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 134 ||  
  
yamasyā kṛtirākhyātaṃ bhīmarūpaṃ prajāpate |  
  
|| nir-ṛti ||  
  
dvibhujañca dvinetrañca kṛṣṇavarṇa samāyutam |  
hemavastraparidhānaṃ khaḍgastāṭakasaṃyutam ||  
  
naravāhanasaṃyuktaṃ daṃṣṭrālocanakantathā |  
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ rākṣasaṃ rūpamucyate || 135 ||  
  
|| varuṇan ||  
  
śaṅkha kundendudhavalo dvibhujāñca dvinetrakam |  
sarvābharaṇa saṃyuktaṃ kuṇḍalābhyāṃ virājitam ||  
  
savye pāśābhayaṃ vāme makarasya tu vāḍanam |  
  
p. 116)  
  
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ varuṇasyākṛtirucyate || 136 ||  
  
|| vāyu ||  
  
kṛṣṇavarṇadvinetrañca vītabhūtasavikramam |  
dvipādaṃ śuklavastrañca dvihastañca tathaiva ca ||  
  
savye kuśavahaṃ vāme pralambakaṭakaṃ vahan |  
miśravarṇāmbarā yukto mṛgārūḍho suyauvanām || 137 ||  
  
vāyurūpamiti khyātaṃ vāyusyā kṛtirucyate |  
  
|| kuberan ||  
  
dvibhujā ca trinetrā ca śvetavarṇasamāyutam |  
śuklavastraṃ paridhānaṃ saratnamakuṭānvitam ||  
  
gadāyā savyahaste tu nidhivāme tathaiva ca |  
aśvavāhana saṃyuktaṃ kuberasyā kṛtirucyate || 138 ||  
  
|| īśānam ||  
  
caturbhujaṃ triṇetrañca śuklavarṇaṃ suyauvanam |  
śuklayajñopavītañca vṛṣārūḍhaṃ suśāntakam ||  
  
kapardibhasmaliptāṅgaṃ taruṇendu vibhūṣitam |  
śūlañcābhaya hastañca mṛgaṭaṅka tathaiva ca ||  
  
vāme dakṣiṇe dhārya vyāghracarmāmbarānvitam |  
  
p. 117)  
  
aiśānyākṛtirākhyātaṃ dvibhujaṃ vāpi dhārayet || 139 ||  
  
|| brahmā ||  
  
brahmācaturmukhaḥ pītaścaturdordaṇḍamaṇḍitaḥ |  
srukdaṇḍākṣasruvañcaiva kirīṭīhaṃsavāhanam || 140 ||  
  
|| viṣṇu ||  
  
viṣṇuścaturbhujo māli śaṅkhacakragadābjadhṛk |  
nīlāmbuda pratīkāśo garuḍāsana saṃsthitam ||  
  
dvinetraṃ dvibhujāssarve karaṇḍamakuṭānvitam |  
kṛtāñjali puṭovāpi padmaṃ daṃṣṭrā samanvitam || 141 ||  
  
cakraśūlaṃ tathā khaḍgaṃ aṅkuśaṃ vajradaṇḍakam |  
ekāsyandvibhujaṃ vāme kaṭirdakṣiṇake kare || 142 ||  
  
icchājñāna kriyāśakti rūpaśaktidharaṃ bhaje |  
  
|| rathadhyānam ||  
  
cakrāñca sūrya candraiśca paścāt brahmamayaṃ bhavet |  
tatpaścāt pīṭhameva syāt viṣṇuśaila gajantathā ||  
  
sarvadeveṣu pādañca tatpaścādbhuvanantathā |  
nakṣatraṃ randhramevaṃ syāt nāgañca sūtrabandhanam ||  
  
śikharaṃ niṣkalaṃ vyomaṃ vedāṅgaṃ rathasūtrakaiḥ |  
  
p. 118)  
  
bhaktānāṃ pañcabhūtaiśca pratigrāhyaṃ ṛṣaṃ tathā |  
tatkartu rudramevaṃ syāt dhyāyedeva rathantathā ||  
  
gambhīra brahmaṇāñcaiva śikhāyajñopavītinam |  
sarvābaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ yauvanaṃ śyāmavarṇayet || 143 ||  
  
abhayaṃ ūruhastañca namaskārāñjali hastakam |  
  
|| gopuradhyānam ||  
  
dvārañca brahmadaivatyaṃ nilāviṣṇutathaiva ca |  
nālaṃ kumbheṣu rudrañca śilā iṣṭiñca dārukaiḥ ||  
  
sarvadeva ṛṣiñcaivā vasudhairasañca śaktiṣu |  
sarvatantra vidhānañca bhakaiśca gaṇabhūtakaiḥ ||  
  
śṛṅgārañcāralaṅkṛtya nakṣatrañca samārabhet |  
iti gopurarūpañca netrañca śiranāsiṣu || 144 ||  
  
|| stūpidhyānam ||  
  
upānaṃ pātukañcaiva jagatīṃ jaṅghameva ca |  
bālaprastharasaṃyuktaṃ galaṃtrīpasya saṃyutam ||  
  
śikharaṃ pradeśe makuṭaṃ stūpigopurameva cā |  
vimānaṃ bimbasaṃyuktaṃ dhyānamāvāhanantathā || 145 ||  
  
p. 119)  
  
|| rāvaṇadhyānam ||  
  
daśāsyaṃ kālavarṇañca kopāgninetrameva ca |  
mahābhīṣaṇa rūpañca ghoradaṃṣṭrādharoṣṭhakam ||  
  
netrañca viṃśatiñcaiva bhujahastañca viṃśati |  
navaratna kirīṭaṃ syāt māṇikya kuṇḍalantathā ||  
  
mahābalasamañcaiva sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
cakraśūlañca daṇḍañca japavaṭaṃ khaḍgameva ca ||  
  
vajrañca tomarañcaiva bāṇamaṅkuśasavyake |  
dhanuḥ kamaṇḍalañcaiva paraśuṃ khaḍgameva ca ||  
  
pāśañca śaktighaṇṭāñca kheṭakaṃ sarpavāmake |  
dhārayedveda viprañca garuḍapakṣadvihastake || 146 ||  
  
ālīḍhakānupādañca rāvaṇāsurameva ca |  
  
śeṣadhyānam  
  
pañcabhūtañca pañcāsyaṃ śvetasūtra putantathā |  
kālodantañca jihvā ca nāsī ca marutāni ca ||  
  
karṇaṃ kubera nai-ṛtyāṃ bhāraṇañcandra samācaret |  
pucchaṃ vedasamudrañca śeṣañca nibhahetakai || 147 ||  
  
|| vyāghradhyānam ||  
  
p. 120)  
  
mukhadantā ca jihvā ca mukharomaṃ tathaiva ca |  
indrāgninai-ṛtyāṃ netrakālī ca bhairavam ||  
  
vārāhi raktacāmuṇḍi jyeṣṭhāreṇukarantathā |  
prajākarṇadvayañcaiva brahmaviṣṇuśca pucchakam ||  
  
vaktrañca sarvaśāstreṣu śarīraṃ munidevatam |  
jīvamanmathavedā ca iti vyāghra svarūpakam ||  
  
iti vyāghrāyarūpantu buddhimān deśikottamaḥ || 148 ||  
  
|| mūṣikadhyānam ||  
  
jihvādantañca vādyañca mukhañca nai-ṛtintathā |  
netrañcaiva divārātriṃ karṇañca vāyudevatā ||  
  
gātrañca bhuvanāṇḍaṃ syāt romaṃ vidyādharairmuniḥ |  
pucchaṃ phaṇi anantañca caturvedaṃ catuṣpadam || 149 ||  
  
jīvaṃ syādbrahmaviṣṇuñca iti mūṣikameva ca |  
  
|| haṃsadhyānam ||  
  
netrañca dharmakīrtiñca āsyaṃ parvatiyaiva ca |  
pādadvayañcandrasūryaṃ ca jīvaṃ sthāvara jaṅgamam || 150 ||  
  
haṃsadhyānañca vidhivat buddhimān deśikottamaḥ |  
  
p. 121)  
  
|| gajadhyānam ||  
  
śiramastakavighneśaṃ jihvādaṃṣṭrañca ṣaṇmukham |  
śuṇḍahastamitaṅgī ca śrotraṃ kāmāridurgikā ||  
  
netraṃ arundhati jyeṣṭhā sarvaloka vapu tathā |  
brahmāviṣṇuśca indrañca ṛṣīñca catuṣpādaṃ tathaiva ca || 151 ||  
  
|| siṃhadhyānam ||  
  
mukhañca vīrabhadraṃ syāt netrañca agni nai-ṛte |  
dantañca aṣṭaśailañca jihvāyāṃ kālireva ca ||  
  
romadeha ṛṣisuraiyamavāyu catuṣpade |  
pucchāṃ śvetī tathaivā ca jīvaṃ prāṇañca lakṣmi ca |  
iti siṃhasamākhyātaṃ buddhimān deśikottamaḥ || 152 ||  
  
|| maṇṭapadhyānam ||  
  
śaktī śūlā ca mālā ca abhayaṃ dakṣiṇe kare |  
vajra cakrañca pāśañca pustakaṃ vāmahastake ||  
  
ekavaktrantriṇetrañca sukhāsana manoharam |  
sarvālaṅkāra saṃyuktaṃ dhyāyenmaṇṭapa rūpiṇīm || 153 ||  
  
|| ṣoḍaśagaṇapati dhyānam ||  
  
vighneśvarar-  
  
pāśāṅkuśe bhrama kulādantaṃ  
  
p. 122)  
  
pañcāskaraṃ padmastriyāṅkulipyām |  
pītaprabhaṃ kalpataroruhastaṃ bhavāminṛtto bhavataṅgaṇeśam || 154 ||  
  
karastha kadalīcūtaṃ panaseṣutamodakam |  
bālasūryaprabhaṃvande evaṃ bālagaṇādhipam || 155 ||  
  
navakuṅkumapaṅkīlakucasthali laṃbita cambakalhāralatām |  
maṇinūpura sañcitamañjupadāṃ praṇamāmi sutāgirirājasutām ||  
  
malaughālendu ratnaṃ smarabhujamanalaṃ bālenetregalārtho |  
devotsādaṃ karālaṃ saśaradimathanāt jṛmbhitaṃ kālakūṭam ||  
  
kalyāṇādriṃ hariṣundṛhāṇāva śiraṃkālanāśañca śūlam |  
ṇubje dhatte jagatīḥ paraśivaḥ pātusarveśvaronaḥ || 157 ||  
  
īśānaṃ sphaṭikābhamūrdhvavadanaṃ yatkuṅkumābhaṃ mukhaṃ   
pūrvantatpuruṣānanaṃ jananibhaṃ jāmyantaghorānanam ||  
aurityaṃ kusumaṃ japāsusadṛśaṃ vāmantathā cottare  
sadyojātamukhantu paścimadale gokṣīra tulyaprabham || 158 ||  
  
sumukhaścekadantaśca vimalo gajakarṇikaḥ |  
  
prathamaṃ bālavighneśo dvitīyaṃ taruṇo bhavet |  
tṛtīyaṃ bhaktavighneśo caturtho vīravighnataḥ ||  
  
p. 123)  
  
pañcamaṃ śaktivighneśo ṣaṣṭhaṃ dhvajavināyakam |  
saptamaṃ piṅgalordeve aṣṭamogviṣṭanāyakaḥ ||  
  
navamaṃ vighnarāja syāt daśamaṃ vipranāyakaḥ |  
ekādaśantu herambo dvādaśaṃ lakṣmināyakaḥ ||  
  
triyodaśaṃ mahāvighnaṃ bhuvaneśa caturdaśā |  
pañcādaśantu nṛttākhyaṃ ṣoḍaśodhva gaṇādhipaḥ ||  
  
|| bālagaṇapati ||  
  
karastha kadalīcūtaṃ panasekṣutamodakam |  
bālasūrya prabhaṃ vande devaṃ bālagaṇādhipam || 1 ||  
  
|| taruṇagaṇapati ||  
  
pāśāṅkuśāpūpa kapittha jambhū phalantilā pūpamapitsahaste |  
ya devatāya taruṇāruṇābhaṃ pāyātsa yuṣmāṃstaruṇo gaṇeśaḥ || 2 ||  
  
|| bhaktagaṇapati ||  
  
nālikerāmbukadalī galapāyasadhāriṇām |  
śaratśaśāṅka saṃkāśaṃ bhaje bhaktagaṇādhipam || 3 ||  
  
|| vīragaṇapati ||  
  
bhetālaśaktiśarakārmuka carmakhaḍgaṃ

p. 124)  
  
śūlañca dantaparaśu dhvajamudvadantaṃ vīraṃ gaṇeśamaruṇaṃ satataṃ   
smarāmi |  
  
|| śaktigaṇapati ||  
  
āliṅgya devīṃ haritāniṣaṇṇaṃ parisphurasṛṣṭakaṭinniveśam |  
sandhyāruṇaṃ pāśasṛṇīvahantaṃ bhayāpahaṃ śaktigaṇeśamīḍe || 5 ||  
  
|| dhvajagaṇapati ||  
  
yaṃ postakākṣaguṇadaṇḍakamaṇḍula śrīnirvṛtyamānakara   
bhūṣaṇaminduvarṇa   
stambhe ramānana catuṣṭayaśobhamānaṃ tāṃ vismare dhvajagaṇādhipateṣu   
dhanya || 6 ||  
  
|| piṅgalagaṇapati ||

|| ucchiṣṭagaṇapati ||

|| vināyakar ||

|| kṣipragaṇapati ||

p. 125)

herambagaṇapati

|| lakṣmigaṇapati ||

|| mahāgaṇapati ||

|| vighneśvarar ||

|| ūrdhvagaṇapati ||

|| āliṅganagaṇapati ||

|| vighnarājar ||

|| śayanavighneśvarar ||

|| nair-ṛtavighneśvarar ||

p. 129)  
  
mahodaraṃ bṛhatkāyaṃ gajavaktraṃ gajānanam |

|| umāsutar ||

|| ṣaṇmukhavighneśvarar ||

|| vighneśa pratiṣṭhā sthānam ||

|| gaṇapatidhyānam ||

evandhyātvāviśeṣeṇa pūjayevagaṇādhipam || 34 ||  
  
|| vighneśvaran ||  
  
parivārādi saṃyuktaṃ karaṇḍamakuṭānvitam |

etadruvasmarennityaṃ sarvavighnavināyakam |  
  
|| gaṇapati ||  
  
lambodaraṃ śyāma * * * * * * * * mīḍe || 36 ||  
  
|| gaṇapati ||  
  
raktapadmāsanāsī * * * * * * * dhipam || 37 ||  
  
|| vighneśvaran ||

laḍḍukaṃ paraśuṃ vāme savyadantākṣamālikām ||  
  
nāgayajñopavītañca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ||  
  
p. 132)  
  
sarvakāryāṇi siddhyanti vighnarājanamo'stute || 38 ||  
  
|| vighneśvarar ||  
  
unmṛta-amṛtasāraṃ kuñcitāṅghriṃ sureśaṃ
