kanakamaṇivaktra jantaṃ kalpitaṃ saptahastaṃ   
sakalamayaśarīraṃ sāṅkuśaṃ pāśadantam | 39 |||  
  
palagatapadmayugmaṃ padmasiṃhāsanastham |  
  
|| daśavighneśvarālam ||  
  
āmodaśca pramodaśca pramukhodurmukhastathā |  
avighno vighnakartā ca bhakṣestapañcahastayā || 40 ||  
  
gajavaktrogaṇādhīśaḥ daśaite vighnanāyakaḥ |  
  
|| daśavidhavighneśvaravarṇam ||  
  
āmodaśyāmavarṇantu pramodaṃ raktavarṇakam |  
pramukhaṃ sphaṭikābhāsaṃ durmukhasya tu dhūmrakam ||  
  
avighnaṃ pītavarṇañca vighnaṃ raktāñjanaprabham |  
bhakṣyāśipāṇḍurañcaiva pañcahastasukūrpakam ||  
  
gajavaktrādinīlañca gaṇeśaṃ kuṅkumaprabham |  
ityevaṃ daśavighneśaṃ varṇabhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 41 ||  
  
p. 133)  
  
|| hastam ||  
  
āmodaścāṣṭahastañca pramodaṃ ṣaṭbhujānvitam |  
pramukhandvādaśañcaivā durmukhasya daśastyathā ||  
  
caturhastādivighnaśca vighnakartā ca saptakam |  
bhakṣyapriyadvihastañca pañcahasteti pañcakam ||  
  
gajavaktrācaturhasta gaṇeśasya caturbhujam |  
ityevaṃ daśavighneśo hastanirmitameva cā || 42 ||  
  
|| āyudham ||  
  
khaḍgaṃ pāśāṅkuśaṃ cakraṃ gadāśūlañcamodakam |  
daṇḍaṃ bāṇadhanuścaiva phalapadmantathaiva cā ||  
  
bhindipālañcamusalaṃ kheṭakaṃ śaṅkhameva ca |  
śaktimudgarakhaṭvāgaṃ vajranāgabhayāvaram |  
kuṇḍikāṅkuśakūrcañca kapālaṃ japamālikam ||  
  
postakaṃ dantakhaṇḍañca agnisruksruvameva cā |  
śālagāmarujjyanaṃ sarvāyudhasamaprabham ||  
  
ityevaṃ vighnarājasya āyudhasya prakīrtitaḥ || 43 ||  
  
|| netralakṣaṇam ||  
  
ugranetraṃ samaṃnetraṃ raktanetraṃ tathaiva ca |  
  
p. 134)  
  
śāntanetraṃ japannetraṃ viśālaṃ sūkṣmanetrakam |  
etadvighneśanetreṇa lakṣaṇasya prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
|| daśavighneśa āyudhabhedam ||  
  
triśūlaṃ ḍamaruṃ khaḍgaṃ gadākheṭakapālakam |  
pāśāṅkuśañca āmodaṃ āyudhasya prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
modakaṃ mudgarañcaivā phaladantañca padmakam |  
musalasya tu vinyasya amodasyāyudhaṃ dadhaḥ ||  
  
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaṃ tomaraṃ bhindipālakam |  
dhanurbāṇañca khaṭvāṅgaṃ nāgaṃ pāśañca modakam ||  
  
pramukhañcāyudhaṃ proktaṃ sarvakāryeṣu siddhidam |  
salākāgnisudantañca daṇḍaṃ vīṇañca vajrakam ||  
  
śūlābhayavarañcaiva śaktidurmukhameva cā |  
kuṇḍikāṃ daṇḍakūrcañcā japamālāya vighnakam ||  
  
kapitthaṃ sruksruvañcaiva jñānadantañca postakam |  
modakaṃ vighnakartā ca āyudhasya prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
tilamodakadantañca bhakṣyapriyamiti smṛtam |  
pāśāṅkuśakapitthañca apūpaṃ śvetapadmakam ||  
pañcahasteti vinyasya āyudhasya prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
p. 135)  
  
aṅkuśaṃ laḍḍukañcaiva nālikerañca modakam |  
bhajavaktrāyate tubhyaṃ āyudhasya vidhīyate ||  
  
pāśāṅkuśaphalaṃ cūtaṃ raktapadmasya modakam |  
gaṇeśasya tu vinyasya āyudhasya prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
|| vāhanam ||  
  
ārodavyāghravāhantu pramodaṃ siṃhameva ca |  
pramukhaṃ gandhabherañca durmukhasya tu vṛścikam ||  
  
avighnādi gaṇeśāntaṃ mūṣikasya tu vāhanam |  
sarvavighneśayoścaiva pūjayettu samanvitaḥ ||  
  
nadītīre catudvāre sthāpayet tu pramodakam |  
pramukhaṃ kūpatīre tu mahāraṇye tu durmukham ||  
  
avighnaṃ hariramye ca vighneśaṃ bauddhamandire |  
āhatālayate bhakṣyā priyaṃ vakṣyo bhavedbudhaḥ ||  
  
mātrālayānyasetkāre durgānvaya gajastake |  
skandālaye gaṇeśasya sthāpayet sthāpakottamaḥ ||  
  
sarvaśānti samāyuktaṃ sarvavighneśavadbhavet |  
evaṃ lakṣaṇamākhyātaṃ daśavighneśvarasya tu ||   
  
mantroddhāravidhiñcaiva śṛṇuṣva deśikottamaḥ |  
  
p. 136)  
  
dhyānamāvāhanaṃ kṛtvā pūjayeva gaṇādhipam |  
putraśrīdhanadhānyañca sarvasaubhāgyadāyinam ||  
  
manobhīṣṭaphalañcaiva dhyātvāsiddhivināyakam |  
pūjayitvā mahābhāgaṃ gaṇeśaṃ siddhidāyakam ||  
  
sidhyanti sarvakāryāṇi manasā cintitānyapi |  
tenakhyāti trilokena nāmnāsiddhivināyakaḥ ||  
  
kāryā sakalasarveṣu pūjaniryagaṇādhipam |  
vidyārambheṣu kalyāṇaṃ vidyāllābhobhaveddhruvam ||  
  
yatnādau devakāryāṇi yuddhasannāhameva ca |  
ityetat kāryamevantu karṣakoṇavināyakam ||  
  
pratiḥ trisandhyāyāṃ snānakāle japeṣu ca |  
āraṇye corabhītiśca nandimadhye mahājane ||  
  
raṇamādhyāgni madhye ca devadarśanakālayoḥ |  
dhyātvā vināyakañcaivā smaraṇe tu mahāphalam ||  
  
yantra sthāpanakāle ca mantroddhāraṇakālayoḥ |  
tantrastambha pratiṣṭhā ca smaraṇe tu vināyakam ||  
  
ityevantu gaṇeśasya smaraṇasya mahāphalam |  
sarvakāryāṇi sidhyarthaṃ dhyātvā siddhivināyakam ||  
  
p. 137)  
  
namāmi vighnārthamumāsutā pra īṃ namākundendu sarasvatī |  
namāmyahaṃ śrīgurupādapaṅkajannamāmi brahmārarcitaṃ vā śivam ||  
  
|| hariḥ om | śubhamastu ||  
  
jñānaśaktidharaṃ skando devasenāpatintathā |  
subrahmaṇyo gajārūḍhaśśarakānana saṃbhavam ||  
  
kārtikeyaḥ kumāraśca ṣaṇmukhastārakāntakaḥ |  
senāni brahmaśāstā ca vallī kalyāṇasundaraḥ ||  
  
bālaśca krauñca bhettāśikhivāhana eva cā |  
etāni svāmināmāni ṣoḍaśapratyahannaraḥ ||  
  
yaḥ paṭhet sarvapāpebhyo samucyeda mahāmune |  
eteṣāṃ pratirūpāṇāṃ dhyānamāvāhanocyate ||  
  
prathamaṃ jñānaśaktiñca dvitīyaṃ skandameva ca |  
senāni tritiyañcaiva subrahmaṇyacaturthakam ||  
  
pañcamantu gajārūḍho śarakānanaṣaṣṭhamam |  
saptamaṃ kārtikeyañcā kumārañcāṣṭamastathā ||  
  
navamaṃ ṣaṇmukhañcaiva daśamaṃstārakāntaram |  
senānyekādaśaṃ proktaṃ dvādaśaṃ brahmaśāstayoḥ ||  
  
sundarīśatriyodaśyāṃ bālane tu caturdaśā |  
  
p. 138)  
  
pañcādaśaṃ krauñcahāri ṣoḍaśaśśikhivāhanam |  
  
|| śaktidharadhyānam ||  
  
ekavaktraṃ dvinayanaṃ caturdordaṇḍamaṇḍitam |  
śaktivajradharopetaṃ varadābhayapāṇinam ||  
  
kundamandasthitaṃ śāntaṃ kuṇḍalābharaṇojvalam |  
dhyāyen taṃ śarasaṃhāraṃ mayūrārūḍhamavyayam ||  
  
ekāsya dvibhujaṃ vāme kaṭidakṣiṇakekare |  
icchā jñānakriyāśaktirūpaśaktidharaṃ bhavet || 1 ||  
  
|| skandadhyānam ||  
  
kalpadrumaṃ praṇamatāṃ kamalāruṇābhaṃ skandaṃ   
bhujadvayamanāmayamekavaktam |  
kātyāyanaṃ sutamahaṃ kaṭibaddhabālaṃ kaupīnadaṇḍadharadakṣiṇahastamīḍe ||  
  
|| senāpati ||  
  
naumyāditya pradīptaṃ dvidaśanayanaṃ ṣaṇmukhaṃ mandahāsaṃ  
vāmāṅge svastidāyaḥ sarasiruhadhṛtaliṅgitāyaḥ priyāyāḥ |  
uttuṅgorustanāgre vihitakaratalaṃ bhītikheṭāśūlāṃ  
hridinyodīptaśaktiṣvasanaghanagadā kukkuṭābjañca hastām ||  
  
|| subrahmaṇyadhyānam ||  
  
ekavaktraṃ dvidordaṇḍaṃ kaṭibaddhābhayānvitam |  
  
p. 139)  
  
taruṇāruṇa saṃkāśaṃ subrahmaṇyamupāsmahe || 4 ||  
  
|| gajārūḍhadhyānam ||  
  
ekānanandvinayanaṃ varakukkuṭau ca vāmadvaye niśitaśaktyabhayau dvayene |  
bibhrāṇamīśvarasutaṃ tapanāyutāpaṃ nityannamāmigajavāhanamiṣṭasidhyai ||  
  
|| śarakānanaḥ ||  
  
śaktiṃ kheṭañca khaṇṭāṃ dhvajasarasije kukkuṭaṃ prāsadaṇḍaṃ  
ṭaṅkaṃ bāṇaṃ varadamabhayaṃ kārmukañcordvahastam |  
pītaṃ saumyaṃ dvidaśanayanaṃ kekahaṃsayyamitrāṃ-  
sābhiḥ pūjyaṃ śaravaṇabhavaṃ ṣaṇmukhaṃ bhāvayāmi || 6 ||  
  
|| kārtikeyar ||  
  
varadakuliśakheṭaṃ vāmahastatriye ca dadhatamabhayaśakti khaḍgamanyatreḥ  
taruṇaravisamābhaṃ sādhubhiḥ pūjyamānaṃ kamalavadanaṣaṭkaṃ kārtikeyanna ||  
  
|| kumārar ||  
  
savyadvaye niśitaśaktisimādadhānāṃ vāmadvayebhimata kukkuṭakheṭakañca |  
vallīpatiṃ vibudhalocana pūrṇacandraṃ kalhāranīradatanuṃ kalaye kumāram ||  
  
|| ṣaṇmukham ||  
  
śaktiṃ śarañcakhaḍgañca cakrapāśo'bhayantathā |  
kuliśañca dhanuḥ kheṭaṃ kukkuṭaṃ sāṅkuśaṃ varam ||  
  
p. 140)  
  
mayūravāhanañcaivā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam |  
gajāyai gajavallī ca vāmadakṣiṇameva ca ||  
  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
sarvāyudha jayaṃ vande ṣaṇmukhastasya rūpakam || 9 ||  
  
|| tārakāntakam ||  
  
varadamaṅkuśadhvaje ca kaṭakau cāpavajrakam ||  
  
abhayaṃ pāśakhaḍgañca kramusalaśaktimanviham |  
dvidaśapāṇibhirdadhānaṃ aruṇaṃ koṭisannibham ||  
  
bhajatatārakākāramitrabhayavināśakāraṇam || 10 ||  
  
|| senāpati sameta dhyānam ||  
  
abhayavaradahastaṃ aṅkuśaṃ śaktiśūlaṃ varadakuliśapāśaṃ padmadaṇḍaṃ   
gadāñca |  
dadhatumubhayavakṣaṃ dvādaśāyāmahastaṃ dvidaśakamalanetraṃ   
devasenānyamīḍe || 1 ||  
  
|| brahmaśāstā ||  
  
vāme kare ca yugale varakuṇḍikāñca savyekṣasūtramabhayaṃ dadhataṃ   
viśākham |  
valyāyutaṃ vanajalocanamekavaktraṃ vandāmahe vanajasaṃbhava śāsitāram || 12 ||  
  
|| kalyāṇasundaraḥ ||  
  
hastadvandvekṣamālāmabhayamapi bhṛdāṃ kuṇḍikāṃ śroṇibaddhaṃ  
savye vāme niṣaṇṇaṃ śruvadhṛtividhinā hūyamānena yuktam |  
  
p. 141)  
  
sarvālaṅkārayuktāṃ karakalaśabhṛtāviṣṇunācāruṇābhāṃ   
vallīṃ kalyāṇamūrtiṃ sakalasuragaṇaisthūyamānaṃ prapadye || 13 ||  
  
|| bālasubrahmaṇyam ||  
  
padmasavyakaṭisaṃyutavāmaṃ padmakāntinibha mekhamukhānta |  
bālavṛddhikaramīśvarasūnuṃ bālamunnatamahaṃ praṇato'smi nityam ||  
  
|| krauñcabhedidhyānam ||  
  
abhayamasikapāṇaṃ śaktibāṇañca savye varadakuliśapāpaṃ kheṭakañcāntaṃ |  
dadhatamamarasenānāyakañcāṣṭabāhuṃ kamalavadanaṣaṭkaṃ   
krauñcabhettāramīḍe ||  
  
|| śikhivāhanadhyānam ||  
  
vidrumaprabhameka mukhaṃ vibhuṃ vajraśaktivarābhayapāṇinam |  
devalokaripughnamavighnadaṃ naumirudrabhuvaṃ śikhivāhanam || 16 ||  
  
|| ṣaṇmukham ||  
  
vidrumanibhadvidaśa hastarasavaktraṃ śaktiśarakhaḍgatamabhayadhvajagatā ca   
vāmakaracāpakuliśañca kaṭakaṃ syāt śūlavarapaṅkajasuṣaṇmukhasvarūpa ||  
  
|| nṛttasubrahmaṇyam ||  
  
abhayakaṭakaṭaṅkaṃ mṛgāṅkasya jāhnavī gauripuṣpavaraśyāmam |  
  
skandamupāsmahe || 18 ||  
  
p. 142)  
  
|| kumāradhyānam ||  
  
abhayavaradahastaṃ mekavaktraṃ kumāraṃ varadakaratalābhyāṃ   
vajraśaktindadhāmaṇimakuṭavirājan padmapatraḥ karṇaṃ   
prathamavaruṇavāyusthāpitaṃtatku ||  
  
|| subrahmaṇyam ||  
  
dvihastaṃ yajñasūtrasyo saśikhaḥsahamekhalam |  
kaupīnadaṇḍa yuk savyaṃ vādamāmi kaṭispṛśam ||  
  
dvibhujāñca dvinetrāñca subrahmaṇyañca sundaram |  
padmadhṛk savyapāṇistu itaraśaktidhṛkkarauraḥ || 20 ||  
  
|| bālaskandadhyānam ||  
  
taruṇādityasaṃkāśaṃ saśvadvālaṃ svarūpiṇam |  
caturbhujandvinetrañca karṇayo padmapiṇḍadhṛk ||  
  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ jalaṃkalaśamagrataḥ |  
ratnakuṇḍalasaṃyuktaṃ vajraśakti karadvaye ||  
  
varadābhayasaṃyuktaṃ śaktidvayasamanvitam |  
hārakeyūrasaṃyuktaṃ mayūravāhanantathā || 21 ||  
  
|| subrahmaṇyar ||  
  
caturbhujandvinetrañca karṇayoḥ padmapiṇḍadhṛk |  
nakrakuṇḍalasaṃyuktaṃ samīpe śaktikādvayam ||  
  
p. 143)  
  
dakṣavāmakarāgre tu akṣamālākamaṇḍalum |  
varadābhayayukto vā kaṭisūtrasamanvitam ||  
  
mayūravāhanayuktovāpyathavāyuktapātrakam |  
śaktikāya tato vā'pi triyolakṣaṇamucyate || 22 ||  
  
|| ṣaṇmukham ||  
  
ṣaḍvaktraṃ śikhivāhanaṃ triṇayanaṃ citrāṃbarālaṅkṛtaṃ  
śaktiṃ vajramasiṃ triśūlamabhayaṃ pāśandhanuścakrakam |  
kheṭaṃ kukkuṭamaṅkuśañca varadaṃ dorbhissadānaṃ sadā  
dhyāyed vandita siddhidaṃ skandaṃ surārādhipam || 23 ||  
  
|| bālasubrahmaṇyam ||  
  
caturbhujo bālaveṣo skandaḥ kanakasannibhaḥ |  
śaktikukkuṭahastāśca varābhayakarānvitaḥ || 24 ||  
  
|| kumārar ||  
  
dāḍimī puṣpasaṅkāśaṃ kubjābhaṃ kuṅkumākṛtim |  
ekavaktraṃ caturhastaṃ kaṭibaddhabhayāstakam ||  
  
kamaṇḍalākṣodharañcaiva karaṇḍamakuṭojjvalam |  
hārakeyūrasaṃyuktaṃ kaṭisūtroktabandhanam ||  
  
yajñopavītasaṃyuktaṃ channavīrasamanvitam |  
  
p. 144)  
  
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kumāraṃ śaṅkarātmajam || 25 ||  
  
|| nandakumāram ||  
  
kuṅkumavarṇacaturbhujayuktaṃ śaktidharaṃ varadaṃ kaṭakañca |  
vajravarābhaya dakṣiṇahastaṃ sundaranandana skandakumāram || 26 ||  
  
|| kārtikeya dhyānam ||  
  
gāṅgeyaṃ vahnigarbhaṃ śaravaṇa janitaṃ jñānaśaktiṃ kumāraṃ  
brahmāṇḍaṃ skandadehaṃ guhamacalahitaṃ raudratejassvarūpam |  
senānyantārakāgniṃ gajamukhasahitaṃ kārtikeyaṃ ṣaḍāsyaṃ   
subrahmaṇyaṃ mayūraṃ dhvajarathasahitaṃ devadevannamāmi || 27 ||  
  
|| kumāradhyānam ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇāntara śaktipatrabhuvanaṃ tanmantra sañjīvanaṃ   
śaivajyotiśiraḥ karotu na puruṣaṃ dharmānuddhārāmṛtam |  
vijñānaṃ viduṣāṃ viśuddhahṛdayaṃ vibhājamānaṃ śubhaṃ  
traikoṇācala devadevatanayaṃ vande kumāraṃ prabhum || 28 ||  
  
|| śakhaṇodbhavam ||  
  
kanakakuṇḍalamaṇḍitaṣaṇmukhaṃ vivatarāji virājita sevitam |  
niśitaśastra śarāsavadhāriṇaṃ śakhaṇodbhavamīśasutaṃ bhaje || 29 ||  
  
|| senānikalyāṇa rūpadhyānam ||  
  
p. 145)  
  
pītavarṇandvinetrañca ekavaktrandvihastakam |  
navaratnakirīṭañca svarṇamābharaṇantathā ||  
  
skandasya vāmahastena senānyai dakṣahastakam |  
tarjanyāṅgulasaṃyuktaṃ kaniṣṭhāṅgulisaṃyutam ||  
  
aṅgulyāssvarṇavalayaṃ kaṭakaṃ vāmahastake |  
skandasya dakṣahastena śvetapadmasamanvitam ||  
  
skandaṃ kirīṭasvarṇañca hāramābharaṇantathā |  
skandaṃ pītāmbarañcaiva senānyai rajanītrakam ||  
  
jājī campakamevantu nīlotpalañca pāṭali |  
ityevaṃ puṣpamālāyāṃ senānyai skandadhāriṇam ||  
  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇaśobhitam |  
brahmādi devatāścaiva caturvedaśruti smṛtam ||  
  
ṛṣiṇāṃ gaṇasaṃyuktaṃ puṣpavarṣamiti smṛtam |  
yakṣaḥ kinnaragandharva siddhavidyādharaiḥ surān ||  
  
gītavādyādighoṣañca nṛttasaṅgītameva ca |  
skandasenānya pādena indrasaṃmṛjyameva ca ||  
  
indrāṇī svarṇakumbhañca gandhodakamiti smṛtam |  
pārvatī caiva rudraśca saccidānandarūpakam || 30 ||  
  
p. 146)  
  
|| subrahmaṇyar ||  
  
vande sindhūrakāntiṃ śaravaṇabhavaṃ śrīmayūrādhirūḍhaṃ   
ṣaḍvaktraṃ devasenā madhuriputanayā vallabhaṃ dvādaśākṣam |  
śaktibāṇaṃ kṛpāṇaṃ dhvajamapi ca gadāṃ cābhayaṃ savyahastaṃ  
cāpaṃ vajraṃ sarojaṃ kaṭakamapivaraṃ śūlamanyerdadhānam || 31 ||  
  
|| subrahmaṇyar ||  
  
sindhūrāruṇamindukāntivadanaṃ keyūrahārādibhiḥ   
divyairābharaṇairvibhūṣitakaraṃ svargādi saukhyapradam |  
ambhojābhaya śaktikukkuṭadharaṃ raktāṅgarāgāṃ śubhaṃ   
subrahmaṇyamupāsmahe praṇamatāṃ iṣṭārtha siddhipradam || 32 ||  
  
|| brahmasutadhyānam ||  
  
indurūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi vākkāyuta sutejase |  
vyākhyāna mudrāsahitaṃ devasaṃkhaissamāhitam ||  
  
vāmadakṣiṇapārśve tu gajavallisamanvitam |  
āyudhānāñca bṛndaiśca tejo bradaiśca bhāsvaram ||  
  
sādhakānāñca sarveṣu miṣṭārtha phaladāyakam |  
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kiñcit prahasitānanam || 33 ||  
  
|| skandar ||  
  
p. 147)  
  
varadaṃ kaṭibaddhañca abhayaṃ śaktivajrayoḥ |  
śikhināṃ śaktisahitaṃ skandaṃ ekañca vigraham || 34 ||  
  
|| bālasubrahmaṇyar ||  
  
kamaṇḍulākṣamālāñca abhayaṃ varadantathā |  
kaupīnaṃ samapādañca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ||  
  
pītāṅgaṃ suprasannaṃ syāt kirīṭaṃ ratnakuṇḍalam |  
śuklayajñopavītañcā kṛpāluṃ subrahmaṇyakam || 35 ||  
  
senāpati sureśañca harasūnusurāgrajaḥ |  
subrahmaṇyaḥ kumāraśca ṣaṇmukhasya prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
|| ṣoḍaśamūrtiphalam ||  
  
jñānenabrāhmaṇañcaivā skandaṃ prajanavarcasam |  
senānyai'dhipatyaiśca subrahmaṇyañca saundaram ||  
  
gajārūḍhaṃ vivāhañca śarakānanaputrakam |  
kārtikeyañca śauryañca kumāraṃ bahusaṃpadam ||  
  
ṣaṇmukhaṃ bandhuvargañca rājasaṃ tārakārakam |  
naravāhana senānye brahmaśāstā ca vaidyakam ||  
  
kalyāṇasundaraṃ vidyāṃ rājavaśyena bālakam |  
dhānyaputraṃ krauñcahāri jayañca śikhivāhanam ||  
  
p. 148)  
  
ityevaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ devaṃ sarvalokajayapradam |  
dharmārthakāmyamokṣañca sāyujyaṃ sarvasaṃpadam ||  
  
sarvapāpa harandevaṃ śivasāyujya sampadam |  
oṃ jagadbhuve namaḥ | vacat bhuve namaḥ |  
viśvabhuve namaḥ | bhavadbhuve namaḥ | rudrabhuve namaḥ |  
  
jagadbhuvo niṣaṭkañca śivatattvasvarūpakam |  
pūrvādiṣu mukhaicaiva arcaye tu bhavanti hi ||  
  
ityevaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ nāmnāṃ kumbhabiṃbantathaiva ca |  
paṭe vā citramevantu vigrahañcakrameva cā ||  
  
sarvasyānupa mevantu tathā dhyānaṃ tathaiva ca |  
dharmārtha kāmyamokṣārthaṃ sāyujyaṃ sarvasampadam ||  
  
apamṛtyuvināśañca āraṇye bhayanāśanam |  
kṣayābhasmādi kuṣṭādi tāpa jvaranivāraṇam ||  
  
agniśatrubhayaṃ hanti sarvalokaika vaśyakam |  
sarvadāridrya śamanaṃ putrapautrābhi vardhanam ||  
  
sarvakārya jayaṃ vande ṣoḍaśadhyānamarcayet |  
iti dhyātvā mahāsenaṃ namaskṛtvā punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
sādhu vāsādhuvatkarmāyadvadācārite mayā |  
  
p. 149)  
  
tatsarvaṃ devadeveśa guheṇārādhanaṃ param |  
dhyātvā phalantu yaḥ sarvaṃ ātmanā saha buddhimān ||  
  
tadbhaktyā cintayennityaṃ trikālaṃ vā paṭhejjapam ||  
  
śrīkumāragurucaraṇāravindābhyānnamaḥ |  
caturbhujantriṇetrañca kapālaṃ śūlameva cā ||  
  
dakṣiṇe'bhayaṭaṅkaṃ syā vāme parśve samanvitaḥ |  
jaṭāmakuṭa saṃyuktaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam ||  
  
tasyaiva dakṣiṇe pārśve yamunāñcaiva kārayet |  
dvibhujañca dvinetrāñca śyāmavarṇa samanvitam ||  
  
kūrmāsana samāyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
pūrṇakumbhasya vāme tu utpalaṃ savyahastake ||  
  
yamunāyāṃ svarūpantu sarvāvayavasundarīm |  
dvārasya vāmapārśve tu mahākālaimunastathā ||  
  
yamunāñca mahākālīṃ tasya vāme tu pūjayet |  
  
|| pañcaviṃśati vigraham ||  
  
prathamaṃ somadhārī ca dvitīyaṃ umayā saha |  
tṛtīyaṃ vṛṣabhārūḍhaṃ caturthannṛttarūpakam ||  
  
vivāhaṃ pañcamañcaivā ṣaṣṭhaṃ bhikṣāṭanaṃ bhavet |  
  
p. 150)  
  
kāmārī saptamaṃ vidyāt kālāricāṣṭamaṃ bhavet |  
navamaṃ tripurāriṃ syāt jalandharavadho daśā ||  
  
ekādaśaṃ gajāri syāt dvādaśaṃ vīrabhadrakam |  
trayodaśaṃ harerarthaṃ ardhanāri caturdaśam ||  
  
pañcādaśaṃ kirātaṃ syāt kaṅkālaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ bhavet |  
caṇḍeśānugrahañcaivā tatassaptadaśo bhavet ||  
  
viṣāpahāriṇīñcaiva aṣṭādaśamiti smṛtam |  
cakrapradāna rūpantu ekonaviṃśatistathā ||  
  
vighnaprasādādviṃśañca somāskandeka viṃśati |  
dvāviṃśadeka pādaṃ syāt trayoviṃśassukhāsanam ||  
  
dakṣiṇāmūrti rūpantu caturviṃśa prakīrtitam |  
liṅgodbhavasya rūpantu pañcaviṃśatimeva cā ||  
  
ete maheśarūpantu mūrtibhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
  
|| somadhāri dhyānam ||  
  
vipulavadananetraṃ saumyaśṛṅgārabhāvaṃ   
abhayavaradahastaṃ candrabimbāṅgamaulim |  
ṛjutanu samapādaṃ sthānakaṃ vidrumābhaṃ   
paraśuhariṇadhāriṃ padmapīṭhoparistham || 1 ||  
  
p. 151)  
  
|| umayāsahitam ||  
  
dhavalābhasukhāsana devi yutaṃ hariṇī mṛgaṭaṅkabhayaṃvaradam |  
samukhīkalamutpala dṛśyadharaṃ umayāsaha devasvarūpamidam || 2 ||  
  
|| vṛṣārūḍham ||  
  
savye sādvakrakuṇḍānvita kaṭakakaro gopate mastakaste  
vāme syārthaṃ savakṣaṃ aparakarayutaṃ ṭaṅkakṛṣṇaṃ dadhānam |  
pṛṣṭhe syākṣā prasannaṃ triṇayanalasitaṃ baddhaveṇī kirīṭaṃ   
savye gauryāsametaṃ bhajataśubhakaraṃ taṃ vṛṣārūḍhamīśam || 3 ||  
  
|| nṛttamūrti ||  
  
śauryābhasmāradūrdhve sthitapadavilasadvāmamuddhṛtyapādaṃ  
jvālāmālāsumadhye naṭanaphaṇivaśārdūla pādādisevān |  
bhasmoddhūlanamaṅgamālyavilasat vāmedyumāse sitāṃ  
agniṇḍolakarābhayāṃ ḍamarukaṃ dhyātvā naṭeśaṃ bhaje || 4 ||  
  
|| kalyāṇasundaradhyānam ||  
  
sindhūrābhantriṇetrāṃ yugabhujasahitāṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣyaṃ   
divyairvastrāpidhānaṃ jaṭamakuṭadhanuṃ dāmakalhārabhūṣyam |  
śambhundakṣiṇahastapārvatīkaṃ sarvasya saṃgṛhyatām ||  
  
ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgādharaṃ vaśakaraṃ cūḍendubā * * * *   
  
p. 152)  
  
devandakṣiṇa hastapārvatiyutaṃ śrībhūmi devyāśriyaṃ   
dhātāvahni purātanaṃ sthitihariṃ vāmeśahastodakam |  
ghoṣairvādya sageyanṛttavilasan sarvādi devāt ṛṣīn   
stutyā puṣpakṛtāñjaliṃ parivṛtaṃ kalyāṇamūrtiṃ bhajet || 5 ||  
  
|| bhikṣāṭanar ||  
  
bhasmoddhūlanamaṅgavidrumanibhaṃ pādāmbujaṃ pādukaṃ   
rudrākṣeṇa viśeṣabhūṣaṇayutaṃ śeṣasya kaṭyobhujobhāvṛtam |  
hastau śūlakapālamanyaḍamaruṃ dūrvāmṛgasyāsanaṃ  
yānantāgna vikīrṇakeśa sahitaṃ bhikṣāṭanaṃ devatām || 6 ||  
  
|| kāmāridhyānam ||  
  
purate sahamumayā sthitamañjalitaṃ paramamadanaṃ dahanaṃ vapuṣam |  
aparasya nirīkṣaṇamīśamukhaṃ taddakṣiṇayogamivānyaguṇam || 7 ||  
  
|| kālāntakar ||  
  
bandhūkābhantriṇetrāṃ yugabhujasahitāṃ śūlamuddhṛtyahastaṃ   
ṭaṅkaṃ sūcivaraṃ supāśasayutaṃ bhīṣmadaṃṣṭraṃ suvaktram |  
pādau kuñcitavāmamuddhṛtatalaṃ kālasya vakṣasthalaḥ   
laṅghyaṃ bhinnajaṭādharaṃ praṇamatāṃ kālāntaṃ daivatām || 8 ||  
  
|| tripurāntakaḥ ||  
  
p. 153)  
  
ekavaktraṃ samāyuktaṃ caturhastasamanvitam |  
dhanurbāṇasamāyuktaṃ mṛgaṃ paraśudhāriṇam || 9 ||  
  
umayāsahitaṃ vāme devaṃ vai tripurāntakam |  
  
|| jaladharam ||  
  
raktābhamugra tathā bhavadastu tasya ṭaṅkañca pañcahariṇī hatapallavedhṛk  
pūrve jaladharaśayārhata larghyacakraṃ yuktaṃ jaṭādharabhānuṃ vahnisvarūpaka |  
  
|| gajasaṃhāram ||  
  
sthitvā hastiśirordhvasavyacaraṇaṃ vāmāṅghrivaktroddhṛtaṃ   
pucchordhvāvṛta carmamuddhṛtakaraṃ śūlāsibhaṃ śṛṅgakam |  
pāśaṃ kheṭakapālamaṣṭabhujayuk bhīṣmānanena prabhā  
vāme gauri bhayāmukhī sutayutaṃ mūrdhvasya hastaṃ haram || 11 ||  
  
|| vīrabhadradhyānam ||  
  
śvetātkāraṃ śeṣabhūṣaṇadharaṃ vinyastavīṇādharaṃ  
ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgādharaṃ karayuge śārdūlacarmāmbaram |  
ardhonmīlanalocana triyayutaṃ maulījaṭābandhakaṃ  
vande santata vīrabhadracaraṇa ambhoruhaḥ pāhimām || 12 ||  
  
|| harirardhadhyānam ||  
  
vāmapārśve hariṃ kuryāt dakṣiṇe rudrameva ca |  
  
p. 154)  
  
haricakradharañcaiva rudraṃ triśūladhāriṇam |  
pītāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ vyāghracarmāmbaraṃ haram ||  
  
viṣṇuṃ kirīṭasaṃyuktaṃ śaṅkarantu jaṭānvitam |  
tulasya mālinaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ syād bilvamālinam ||  
  
viṣṇubhūṣaṇanīlañca śaṅkaraṃ sphaṭikantathā |  
pādukopari pādau ca sarvabhūta samāvṛtam || 13 ||  
  
sarvālaṅkāra saṃyuktaṃ śaṅkarārdheha viṣṇunām |  
  
|| ardhanāridhyānam ||  
  
dakṣiṇe kuñcitaṃ pādaṃ vāmapādaṃ ṛju sthitam |  
madhyakāyāṃ naro nārī kramaṃ kāryaṃ tribhaṅgikam ||  
  
harasya dakṣiṇe haste triśūlamubhayantathā |  
pārvatī vāmabhāge ca padmañca kaṭikāstakam ||  
  
śvetavarṇa harasyantu umāyai śyāmavarṇakam |  
vyāghracarmāmbaraṃ śambhuṃ pītāmbara maheśvarīm ||  
  
harasya dakṣiṇe karṇe sarpakuṇḍala saṃyutam |  
umāyai vāmakarṇena svarṇakuntalameva ca ||  
  
rudrasya bilvamālāyāṃ śaṅkarī jājipuṣpakam |  
śambho jaṭadharañcaivā kirīṭaṃ śaṅkarī tathā ||  
  
p. 155)  
  
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
sarvadevāñjaliñcaiva śaṅkarārdheha pārvatī || 14 ||  
  
|| kirātadhyānam ||  
  
raktāṅgaṃ dvibhujaṃ tathā śaradhṛtaṃ muktālakaṃ saṃsthitaṃ  
mugrākṣadvayasaṃyutaṃ vipulavaktra vakṣavistīrṇakam |  
muktāpuṣpa sakarṇa bhīṣaṇadharaṃ śārdūlacarmāmbaraṃ   
baddhau pāda virājitodaramabhidhyāyet kirātavaram || 15 ||  
  
|| kaṅkāladhyānam ||  
  
bhasmāṅkalena karaṃ tripuṇḍravilasat sindhūracitrānvitaṃ   
ḍakkāvāmakareṣu savyapraharaṃ carmāmbaraiśśobhitam |  
śūlā * syalambitakaraṃ cūḍendubaddhasphurat  
yānaṃ sendrapure caroṣadhisure bhūtādi līlāvṛtam || 16 ||  
  
|| caṇḍeśānugrahadhyānam ||  
  
caṇḍeśaṃ pītavastraṃ karatalayugalairnetra yugmañca manye  
vāmāṃ savyakṛtāñjali karau devāsanāyostitam |  
devīṃ devasukhāsanena vilasaddeveśayormadhyame  
caṇḍeśānmakuṭasya śambhukaratalaḥ dhṛtvā sutānugraham || 17 ||  
  
|| viṣāpaharaṇam ||  
  
p. 156)  
  
bhānunibhavedakara vahninayanaṃ syāt  
dakṣiṇekare tu viṣa bhakṣaṇa varadastam |  
raktavasanānvita jaṭālambayuktaṃ  
bhīmavadanānvita viṣāpahararūpam || 18 ||  
  
|| cakrapradānam ||  
  
vidyādvādaśa pure hṛdāñjali kṛtau devasya pādābjayoḥ  
paśyākṣān kaṭakāsitena phalasat maulyāmbarākaustubham |  
sthitvā devaruṇābhaśobhita tanuṃ viṣṇuśca padmojvalaṃ  
ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgaṃ varābhayakaraṃ cakraprasādaṃ haram || 19 ||  
  
|| vighnaprasādadhyānam ||  
  
vighneśaṃ raktavarṇaṃ bhujagasahitaṃ śyāmavarṇantriṇetraṃ   
ikṣuḥ kalpasudhārayeka daṇḍaka bahuṃ hastasya prāpādharaṃ |  
vighnaprasādaṃ haram * * * * * * * * *   
  
|| somāskandadhyānam ||  
  
udyadbhānunibhāṃśatakṣara yugaṃ keyūra hārādibhiḥ   
divyairvastrābhidhānairjaṭamakuṭalasat netratrayaṃ śobhitam |  
vāme gauriyutaṃ sukhāsanabhayo madhye kumārasthitaṃ  
somāskandeśarūpaṃ mṛgavaradabhayāṭaṅkaṃ bibhrāṇamevam ||  
  
p. 157)  
  
|| ekapādaḥ ||  
  
dhavalābhasvarūpamaheśaguṇaṃ karaṣaṭkalocanānandayutam |  
hariṇī mṛgaṭaṅka bhayāvaradaṃ karameva maheśvara mekapadām || 22 ||  
  
|| sukhāsana dhyānam ||  
  
aruṇābhasubhasma vilocanasruk hariṇī mṛgaṭaṅkabhayāvaradam |  
karamevaruṇāmbaraśobhalasat guṇayet sukhāsanarūmipadam ||  
  
|| dakṣiṇāmūrtidhyānam ||  
  
jānūrdhvekapādaṃ padamidaṃ bhasmare dehaniyaṃ  
sthitvā nyagrodhamūle munijanamaniśaṃ vedamadhyāvahantam  
vyāghratvagvastramastraṃ sphaṭika japaguṇaṃ jñānamudrākṣamālāṃ  
agniśvetaṃ triṇetraṃ kapilajaṭadharaṃ dakṣiṇāmūrtimīśam |  
  
|| liṅgodbhavadhyānam ||  
  
liṅgaṃ syābhyantare dṛśataharibhuvanādhomukhaṃ syāt   
dvārahantā dūrdhve kamalajanu sāhaṃsarūpān suśobhaiḥ |  
tanmadhye śaivamūrtiṃ sthitamanalanibhaṃ vyāghracarmāmbarasthaṃ  
ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgaṃ varābhayakare liṅgodbhavaṃ pāhimām ||  
  
sundaraṃ somadhārī ca vṛṣārūḍhamumāsaham |  
gaṅgādharañca pañcaite īśānokhya samudbhavā ||  
  
p. 158)  
  
ardhanāri harirārdhaṃ somāskandeśa vighnakam |  
cakraprasādaṃ pañcaite puruṣasyānanodbhavā ||  
  
kāmahā kālahārī ca tripuraghnaśca vīrakam |  
jñānamūrtiṃ gajāri syāt ghoravaktreṣu ca ṣaṣṭakam ||  
  
bhikṣānaṭana kaṅkālaṃ kirātārjunameva cā |  
viṣāpaharaṇaṃ nṛttaṃ vāmavaktre tu pañcakam ||  
  
liṅgodbhavañca caṇḍeśaṃ ekapādaṃ sukhāsanam |  
sadyojātantu vaktrāṇāṃ caturthantu prakīrtitā ||  
  
ityevaṃ pañcaviṃśatyāṃ vigrahasyaṃ puṭasya ca |  
  
|| sṛṣṭi sthitirūpam ||  
  
bhikṣāṭanañca kaṅkālaṃ vīrabhadrantathaiva cā |  
kalyāṇasundarañcaiva candraśekharameva cā ||  
  
gaṅgādharañca pañcaite sṛṣṭirūpaṃ prakīrtitāḥ |  
  
stitirūpam   
  
bhikṣāṭanañca kaṅkālaṃ vīrabhadrantathaiva cā |  
ekapādaṃ vṛṣārūḍhaṃ sthitirūpaṃ prakīrtitam ||  
  
|| saṃhārarūpam ||  
  
gajāritripuraghnaśca manmathasthiti nāśanam |  
  
p. 159)  
  
kaṅkālahāriṇañcaiva dakṣiṇāmūrtireva ca |  
ityevaṃ pañcamūrtiñca saṃhārañceti kathyate ||  
  
|| tirobhāvarūpam ||  
  
kirātaṃ nṛttarūpañca hariharyaviṣāntakam |  
liṅgodbhavasya pañcaite tirobhāvaṃ prakīrtitam ||  
  
|| anugraharūpam ||  
  
cakraprasādavighnaśca caṇḍeśānugrahaṃ bhavet |  
somāskandamiti proktaṃ ardhanārī tathaiva cā || 31 ||  
  
ityevaṃ pañcamūrtiñca anugrahamiti smṛtam |  
ḍamaruṃ sṛṣṭirūpañca aghorañcāgnirūpakam |  
sthiti rūpaṃ bhujaṅgaṃ syāt tirobhāvantu kuñcitam || 32 ||  
  
abhayaṃ anugrahañcaivā pañcakṛtyātmarūpakam |  
aṅkurārpaṇakalyāṇaṃ dhvajārohaṇameva cā |  
rakṣābandhanamityuktaṃ śuddhaṃ?dā hṛdam ||  
  
vāhanotsavasaṃyuktaṃ homakarmaṃ tathaiva ca |  
balibhramaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sthiti karmaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
rajanī cūrṇasaṃyuktaṃ rathārohaṇameva ca |  
kālāgārotsavaṃ kuryāt saṃhārañca prakīrtitam ||  
  
p. 160)  
  
maunotsavaṃ tirobhāvaṃ śaktiyātramanugraham |  
sarve bhaktijanānāntu sevitaṃ bhaktimārgataḥ ||  
  
snānadānantaragataṃ sṛṣṭi sthiti kautuka * |  
bandhayenmiharamāgaruṃ proktaṃ tiraḥ kalpūra lepanam ||  
  
anugrahakaraṃ proktaṃ prabhāte nṛttadarśanam |  
  
|| nityotsava pañcakṛtyam ||  
  
pūjā naivedya sṛṣṭiñca sthiti śrībalināyakam |  
dhūpadīpabalihomaṃ saṃhārañceti kathyate |  
śibikāditirobhāvaṃ kṣetrapālamanugraham ||  
  
ityevaṃ nityapañcaite vidhiḥ kramaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
  
|| īśānamūrdhvamukhadhyānam ||  
  
daśabāhuntriṇetrañca pañcavaktraṃ jaṭādharam |  
vajraṃ śūlañca khaḍgañca śaktiñcābhaya dakṣiṇe ||  
  
pāśāṅkuśaṃ ḍamaruṃ dadhānaṃ varapāṇibhiḥ |  
māṇikya makuṭañcaivā hemāṅgulyādi bhūṣaṇam ||  
  
saumyaṃ sphaṭikavarṇābhaṃ īśānaṃ mūrtirūpakam || 1 ||  
  
|| tatpūrupūrvamukhadhyānam ||  
  
pūruṣaṃ kuṅkumākāraṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbhujam |  
  
p. 161)  
  
savye vāma dadhat ṭaṅkaṃ śūlaṃ ḍamarukantathā |  
gadātriṇetrasaumyañca kiñcitprahasitānanam ||  
  
hemāṅgulīyakañcaivā hemavasottarīyakam |  
muktāhārakirīṭañca māṇikyamaṇibhūṣaṇam ||  
  
ityetatpuruṣamantrassyāt mantramūrti svarūpakam |  
  
|| dakṣiṇe daghoradhyānam ||  
  
aghorandaṣṭriṇaṃ bhīmaṃ raktānanasamaprabham |  
aṣṭabāhuntriṇetrañca caturvaktrañjaṭādharam ||  
  
raktāmbaradharañcaiva raktavastrottarīyakam |  
raktacandanaliptāṅgaṃ raktamālyādibhūṣaṇam ||  
  
śūlabhetālakhaḍgañca dakṣaṃ cakrakare tathā |  
nāgaṃ kheṭañca bāṇañca vismitaṃ vāmapāṇibhiḥ ||  
  
nīlāṅgulīyyakañcaiva nāgayajñopavītinam |  
evaṃ pañcamaghorañca pañcamūrti svarūpakam ||  
  
|| uttare vāmadevadhyānam ||  
  
vāmadevodbhavaṃ raktaṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbhujam |  
mañjīrakaṅkaṇodbhāsi kaṭisūtrottarīyakam ||  
  
raktacandanakañcaiva hemayajñopavītinam |  
  
p. 162)  
  
varadābhayasamāyuktaṃ pāśaṭaṅkakarāmbujam |  
triṇetraṃ trivilāsañca karṇakuṇḍalamaṇḍitam ||  
  
ityevaṃ vāmadevaṃ syāt mantramūrti svarūpakam || 4 ||  
  
|| paścime sadyojātadhyānam ||  
  
śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaṃ caturvaktrañcaturbhujam |  
hārakeyūrakaṭakaṃ kuṇḍalābharaṇojvalam ||  
  
gomedhika kirīṭañca śvetavastrottarīyakam |  
kheṭaṃ ṭaṅkasamāyuktaṃ varadābhayapāṇinam ||  
  
bālenduśekharaṃ vidyāt sadyojātantu mūrtitam || 5 ||  
  
|| pātālamukhadhyānam ||  
  
yaṃvvedādi anantarūpamaguṇaṃ sampūjitāṃ cāmarai  
punnāgārka puṣpavakulaṃ nāgāsurāt pūjite |  
nityaṃ bhānusahasradīptakoṭikiraṇaṃ kālāgnirudropamaṃ   
tatsāhāraharannamāmi satataṃ pātālaṣaṣṭhaṃ mukham || 6 ||  
  
|| pañcamukhasañcāram ||  
  
āsanaṃ śayanaṃ nṛttaṃ ārūḍhaṃ gamanonmate |  
pūjākāle sukhāsīnaṃ anyakāle tu pūrvavat || 7 ||  
  
|| pañcamukhavarṇam ||  
  
p. 163)  
  
īśānaṃ sphaṭikābhāsaṃ pūruṣaṃ kuṅkumaprabham |  
aghoramañjanābhāsaṃ vāmadevantu ratnakam ||  
  
sadyojātantu śvetaṃ syāt pañcavaktreṣu jāyate || 8 ||  
  
|| divyaliṅgadhyānam ||  
  
pīṭhaṃ asyādharitri jaladharakalaśaṃ liṅgamākāśamūrtiṃ  
nakṣatraṃ puṣpamālyāṃ grahagaṇakusumaṃ netracandrārkavahnim |  
kukṣau saptasamudraṃ bhujagiriśikharaṃ saptapātālapādaṃ  
vedaṃ śāstraṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ daśadiśivadanaṃ divyaliṅgannamāmi || 9 ||  
  
|| rudradhyānam ||  
  
pañcānanandaśabhujaṃ pararaktadehaṃ pāśāṅkuśāvaradhṛtakheṭakañca |  
śūlāsibāṇadhanuṣe dadhatañca * * * * * * dāmahe   
varatanuṃ śivayevarudram ||  
  
|| prāsādādhipatidhyānam ||  
  
dvibhujañcādvinetrañca ṭaṅkapāśaśarastathā |  
ugradaṃṣṭri samāyuktaṃ bhīmarūpaṃ mahābalam ||  
  
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam |  
prāsādābhimukhaṃ sarve tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrotkaṭānanam || 11 ||  
  
|| candraśekharadhyānam ||  
  
ekamukhavedakaravidrumasahāsaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgaṭaṅkavaradābhaya catuṣkam  
  
p. 164)  
  
locanantritayasitavastraparidhānaṃ candrayatamauli sahagaurisūnum || 12 ||  
  
|| liṅgodbhavam ||  
  
liṅgaṃ kṛtvotthitobrahma haṃsarūpantathaiva ca |  
viṣṇuṃ varāhakalpantu liṅgasyādhaḥ prakalpayet ||  
  
hṛdayāñjali saṃyuktaṃ brahmāviṣṇudvipārśvayoḥ |  
liṅgamadhye tu kartavyaṃ pūrvavaccandraśekharam || 13 ||  
  
|| āliṅganacandraśekharadhyānam ||  
  
kevalaṅgaurisahitaṃ sahajaṃ gaurisaṃyutam |  
āliṅgañcaikahastena devīṃ devau parasparam ||  
  
(ntu) tamāliṅgamākhyātaṃ evaṃ trividhamucyate || 14 ||  
  
|| parameśvaradhyānam ||  
  
karakalitakapālaṃ kāmanīvāmabhāgaṃ   
śaśiśirasijūṭaṃ nīlakaṇṭhantriṇetram |  
phaṇimaṇikṛtaratnaṃ svarṇadeśekaba * * * * *  
  
|| pārvatīśvaradhyānam ||  
  
śāntaṃ padmāsanasthaṃ śaśidharamakuṭaṃ pañcavaktrantriṇetraṃ   
śūlaṃ vajrañcakhaḍgaṃ paraśumabhayataṃ vāmabhāge vahantam |  
  
p. 165)  
  
nāgaṃ pāśañca khaṇṭāṃ analasahayutaṃ sāṅkuśaṃ vāmabhāge   
nānālaṅkārayuktaṃ sphaṭikamaṇinibhaṃ pārvatīśannamāmi || 16 ||  
  
|| śivadhyānam ||  
  
indunibhapañcamukhahastadaśayuktaṃ śūlamṛgaṭaṅkamahivajramabhayaṃ   
syāt |  
pāśavaradāṅkuśamaṇirdahativāme śvetakamalāsana sadāśivasvarūpam || 17 ||  
  
|| annaliṅgadhyānam ||  
  
caturbhujantriṇetrañca jaṭākhaṇḍendu maṇḍitam |  
hariṇīṭaṅkasaṃyuktaṃ bilvamālāvibhūṣitam || 18 ||  
  
annaliṅgamiti dhyātvā sarvamantreṇapūjayet |  
  
|| dvādaśavigrahabhedam ||  
  
prathamantu mahādevaṃ dvitīyantu maheśvaram |  
tṛtīyaṃ śaṅkarañcaivā caturthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ||  
  
pañcamaṃ śūlapāṇiṃ syāt ṣaṣṭhaṃ kāmāṅganāśanam |  
saptamaṃ devadeveśaṃ śrīkaṇṭhañca tathāṣṭakam ||  
  
navamaṃ īśvaraṃ proktaṃ daśamaṃ pārvatipriyam |  
ekādaśaṃ rudramevantu dvādaśaṃ śivameva cā ||  
  
yete dvādaśabhedāni dhyātvā mantramanusmaran || 19 ||  
  
|| somāskandadhyānam ||  
  
p. 166)  
  
dakṣālambita vāmanidritapadaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ mṛgañcābhayaṃ   
ṭaṅkañcandradharaṃ varañcakaṭakaṃ bibhrāṇakaṃ vāmake |  
vāme lambitanidritānyapadayo devyāyutomadhyatā   
skandenābjakaradvayena sahitaṃ somaṃ guheśaṃ bhaje || 1 ||  
  
|| ṣaṭtriṃśadvigrahabhedam ||  
  
sadāśivaṃ pradhānantu liṅgodbhavamataḥ param |  
candraśekharamākhyātaṃ dakṣiṇāmūrtimeva ca ||  
  
devārtiharaṇaṃ paścāt kālanigrahameva cā |  
kalyāṇasundarañcaivamumayā sahitaṃ tathā ||  
  
somāskandaṃ vṛṣārūḍhaṃ tripurāntakameva cā |  
haryarthamardhanārī ca kaṅkālannṛttarūpakam ||  
  
bhikṣāṭakañcakāmāri aghorāstrasukhāsanam |  
trimūrtimekapādañca gaṅgādharaḥ mataḥ param ||  
  
caṇḍeśānugrahañcaivā ādicaṇḍeśvaraṃ varam |  
gajaghnaṃ brahmamūrtiñca viṣṇumūrtiṃ tathaiva cā ||  
  
skandañca śivasūryañca vighneśaṃ kṣetrapālakam |  
bhairavaṃ bhairavākāraṃ āpamuddhāraṇantathā ||  
  
kirātakaṃ bhaiṣajañcaivā ṣaṭtriṃśadrūpamucyate |  
  
p. 167)  
  
|| sadāśivarūpam ||  
  
pañcāsyaṃ daśahastavakṣanayanaṃ savye'bhayaṃ śūlakaṃ   
vajraṃ śaktibhujaṃṅgamau ca dadhataṃ vāme varaṃ pāśakam |  
ghaṇṭāmaṅkuśa ṭaṅkamarjunakaraṃ prītāsite śobhitaṃ  
śvetaṃ vibhratamānanaṃ hṛdi bhaje sadāśivaṃ vigraham || 1 ||  
  
|| liṅgodbhavam ||  
  
devaṃ garbhagṛhasya mānakalitaṃ liṅgejaṭāśekharaṃ  
kaṭyāsaktakaraṃ sadatradadhataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ mṛgañcābhayam |  
savye ṭaṅkamameya pādamakuṭaṃ brahmācyutābhyāyutaṃ  
ūrdhvādhasthita haṃsakolamamalaṃ liṅgodbhavaṃ bhāvayet || 2 ||  
  
|| candraśekharam ||  
  
aruṇamaṇinibhāṅgaṃ candracūḍantriṇetraṃ hariṇaparaśuvibhrat   
śaktimāliṅgavāme |  
abhayavaradayuktaṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣyaṃ sitakamaladalāgre somadhārisvarūpam || 3   
||  
  
|| dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ ||

savyādhaḥ kṛttivāsaḥ sadanumamatumāṃ dakṣiṇāmūrtidevam || 4 ||  
  
p. 168)  
  
kālanigraham ||  
  
saṃvibhratparaśuñca śūlakamalaṃ * * * * śrīkālanātho'vadat

|| kalyāṇasundaram ||

|| umayāsahitam ||

|| somāskandaḥ ||

|| bhikṣāṭakar ||

karṇekṣiptvāturāṇāṃ kalitakaṃṭhinatanmūlamanyadvihaste |

|| aghorāstram ||  
  
sajalaghanasamānaṃ bhīmadaṃṣṭraṃ triṇetraṃ bhujagadharamaghoraṃ

|| trimūrtiḥ ||  
  
ekāṅghrīṃbja dvipārśve kaṭitaṭighaṭitaṃ svāyutaṃ brahmaviṣṇuṃ

p. 170)

|| ādicaṇḍeśvaraḥ ||  
  
pītābhaṃ trivilocanaṃ śaśiyutaṃ savye'kṣamālādharaṃ   
savyordhve paraśundadhānamapagandhitriśūlaṃ varam |  
savye lambyapadaṃ śṛṇīkṛtapadaṃ vāme tu devyāyutaṃ  
divyaṃ kuṇḍalamaṇḍitānanamahaṃ naumyādi caṇḍeśvaram || 17 ||  
  
|| brahmā ||  
  
pītābhaṃ caturānanaṃ śrutibhujaṃ divyaṃ jaṭāśekharaṃ  
dvinnetraṃ kamayānvitakaraṃ gandhyākṣamālādharam |  
keyūrādibhūṣaṇaṃ sukharaṃ pītāmbarālaṅkṛtaṃ  
haṃsārūḍhamahaṃ visṛṣṭisahitaṃ brahmāṇamīśaṃ bhaje || 18 ||

rājatkuṇḍalaraktadīptimakuṭaṃ śrīviṣṇudevaṃ bhaje || 19 ||  
  
|| rudramūrtiḥ ||

|| skandam ||

|| śivasūryaḥ ||

|| vighneśvaram ||  
  
ekāsyaṃ trivilocanaṃ gajamukhaṃ raktañcaturhastakaṃ   
vāme laḍḍukapāśamanyakarayo dantāṅkuśaṃ bibhratam |  
vāme nidrita pādamanyacaraṇaṃ hyuddhṛtyavinyastakaṃ   
hrasvaṃ tundila śūrpakarṇamaniśaṃ vighneśvaraṃ bhāvayet || 23 ||  
  
|| kṣetrapālam ||  
  
raktajvālajaṭādharaṃ triṇayanaṃ daṃṣṭrākarālānvitaṃ   
haste pāśakapālaśūlaḍamaruṃ dakṣonyataṃ bibhratam |

ghaṇṭāpānasamena jaṃghamamalaṃ kṣetrasyapālaṃ śivam || 24 ||

haste śūlakapālakaṃ ḍamarukaṃ karṇau ca tāṭaṅkinau |  
  
p. 172)  
  
gātraṃ kañcukalambitaṃ satilakaṃ vaktrañca vaktrālakaṃ   
yasyastodharaṇimane dhṛtatanuṃ taṃ bhairavaṃ bhāvayet || 25 ||

nagnoraudraṃ sudaṃṣṭraṃ danujamadahanaṃ bhairavākāramīḍe || 26 ||  
  
|| āpaduddhāraṇam ||  
  
udyadbhāskarasannibhaṃ triṇayanaṃ phullollasatkuntalaṃ

haryakṣājinakañcukaṃ vipanasaṃ jānvantakāntakṣaṇaṃ   
karṇādātmakṛtopavītamaniśaṃ naumyāpaduddhāraṇam || 27 ||

mahāsadāśivañcaivā umāmaheśvaramataḥ param ||  
  
sukhāsīnamumeśañca somāskandaṃ tathaiva ca |

sandhyānṛttaṃ sadānṛttaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ jāhnavī tathā ||  
  
p. 173)

|| sadāśivam ||

|| vṛṣāntikaḥ ||

|| bhujaṅgalalitanṛttadhyānam ||  
  
ekāsyantu caturbhujaṃ triṇayanaṃ vāme ca duttūrakaṃ  
candraṃ patraśikhi prasāritakaraṃ cordhvaṃ padaṃ kuñcitam |  
savye svastikakuṇḍale ḍamarukaṃ gaṅgābhaye bibhrataṃ   
vande nṛttalasadbhujaṃgalalitaṃ bhūtoparisthaṃ śivam ||  
  
|| dhanurbhujaṅgatrāsa nṛttadhyānam ||  
  
dakṣe ḍiṇḍibhujaṅgayuktamapare vahniñca sūcīkaraṃ  
bibhrāṇaṃ karapaṅkajaiḥ samapadaṃ pīṭhesthitaṃ cañcalam |  
saṃyakbandhakapardinaṃ triṇayanaṃ gaṅgenducūḍāśivaṃ  
vande trāsabhujaṅgatāṇḍavapuraṃ śārdūlacarmāmbaram || 14 ||  
  
|| sandhyānṛttam ||  
  
p. 177)  
  
ekaṃ vāmamadasyakuñcitapadaṃ tvanyenabhūtasthito  
vyātyāsena bhujaṅgaprāsārdhaḍamariṃ vyāvartinaḥ pāṇinaḥ |  
ambāvaktra saroruhekṣaṇadiśā sānandamandasthitaṃ   
bhāvyassandhitatāṇḍavaṃ prakaṭayan nāṭye naṭaḥ pāntu naḥ || 15 ||  
  
ekāsyantu caturbhujantriṇayanaṃ vāme ca duttūrakaṃ   
candraṃ patraśikhiprasāritakaraṃ cordhvaṃ padaṃ kuñcitam |  
savye svastikakuṇḍale ḍamarukaṃ gaṅgābhaye bibhṛtaṃ   
bhūtasthāyugapārśvavistṛtajaṭaṃ vande sadā tāṇḍavam || 16 ||  
  
|| kālitāṇḍavam ||  
  
kiñcit kuñcita vāmapādaniciraṃ mañjīramañjitvaṇaṃ   
cañcatkāñcana kiṅkiṇīraṇaraṇat kārāṃśu candrānanam |  
kālītāṇḍavakhaṇḍanaṃ pravilasat raktojvalaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ  
caṇḍaṃ rakṣantu caṇḍikā pratikṛtaṃ sampatkaraṃ tāṇḍavam || 17 ||  
  
|| gaṅgādharaḥ ||  
  
śāntaṃ yogāsanasthaṃ śaśidharamamalaṃ yogapaṭṭāvṛtāṅgaṃ   
ṭaṅkaṃ vyākhye kuraṅgaṃ varamapi dadhataṃ savyamaṅmantriṇetram |  
lambitā cūḍitāṅgaṃ mamalasuradvanditaṃ savyabhāge vahantīṃ  
  
p. 178)  
  
gauryā vāme sametaṃ bhasitasitanuṃ naumigaṅgādhareśam || 18 ||  
  
|| gaṅgāvisarjanam ||  
  
padmasthaṃ śāntarūpaṃ sphaṭikamaṇinibhaṃ bibhrataṃ ṭaṅkaśūlaṃ   
vāme dakṣo'bhayāṅkaṃ parivaradhṛtajaṭaṃ tatsahasrāṃśakoṭyai |  
bhāgīrathyāṃ visṛṣṭiṃ vidadhatamapare sāṃdraṣaṭcakrayuktaṃ   
vande gaṅgāvisargaṃ ruciragirijayā vāmabhāge sametam || 19 ||  
  
|| tripurāntakam ||  
  
raktābhaṃ paripūrṇacandravadanaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ mṛgaṃ kārmukaṃ   
vāme savyakare śarañca dadhataṃ ṭaṅkañca vāme yutam |  
gauryācandrakalādharaṃ hariviriñcādyaissuraissevitaṃ  
hāsāndhapuratriyaṃ triṇayanaṃ devaṃ purārimbhaje || 20 ||  
  
|| kalyāṇasundaram ||  
  
kundābhantarūṇendu cūḍamakuṭaṃ * * * sitamukhaṃ kalyāṇadevaṃ   
bhaje || 21 ||  
  
|| ardhanārīśvaram ||  
  
puṃstrīrūpatanau śaśijaṭā * * * * * * * *   
vande'rdhanārīśvaram || 22 ||  
  
|| gajārīśvaraḥ ||  
  
sthitvāhastiśirastha savyacaraṇaṃ vāmāṅghrivaktroddhṛtaṃ   
  
p. 179)  
  
pucchordhvāvṛtacarmadhṛgyugakaraṃ śūlāsiśṛṅgojvalam |  
vāme kheṭakapālapāśadharakaṃ daṃṣṭrānvitaṃ raktabhaṃ   
devyābhīti guhāptayā ca sahitaṃ devaṃ gajāribhaje || 23 ||  
  
|| jvarāpaghnam ||  
  
tryasyāṃ rudravilocanaṃ guṇabhujaṃ ghoratripādaṃsitaṃ   
savyeḍiṇḍimagarmaprasāritakaraṃ vahniñca vāme dadhat |  
vāme svastikamuddhṛtaṃ padamayovinyasta pādadvayaṃ  
bhasmoddhūlita varṣalambitajaṭaṃ rūpaṃ jvareśaṃbhaje || 24 ||  
  
|| śārdūlaharaḥ ||  
  
pāpāṇḍukañcukantriṇayanaṃ vṛktālakālaṅkṛtaṃ  
śārdūlāsya vihāri hastayugalaṃ savyeddhṛtābjā pare |  
sūcī mūṣikakañcarakṣacaraṇenakrāntatatkandaraṃ  
vande kuñcitamanyapādadadhataṃ śārdūlahārīśvaram || 25 ||  
  
|| pāśupateśvaraḥ ||  
  
vaktrālakaṃ raktatanuntriṇetraṃ śūlābhayaṃ vā ḍamaruñca vāme |  
bibhrāṇamādyaṃ śaśikhaṇḍacūḍaṃ vāme kare pāśupatāstrayuktam ||  
  
savyerjunañcāñjali hastayukta vāmenugrahantamupāsametaṃ  
  
p. 180)

|| kaṅkālaśivam ||

|| haryarthadhyānam ||

|| bhikṣāṭanam ||

bhikṣāṭaneśaṃ bhaje || 29 ||  
  
|| siṃhaghnadevaḥ ||

pakṣadvandvenayuktaṃ sukharavinutaṃ tatpadaṃ vedahastam |  
pādākrānte nṛsiṃhesyuḥ rasividalat pādapadmadvayāḍhyaṃ  
nālaśūlaṃkapālaṃ dadhatamapamo nārasiṃhasya devam || 30 ||  
  
|| caṇḍeśānugrahaḥ ||  
  
tryakṣaṃ candrārdhacūḍaṃ sphaṭikamaṇinibhaṃ ṭaṅkakṛṣṇaṃ dadhānaṃ  
savyelambyāṅghriśobhaṃ śayitavarapadaṃ padmapīṭhoparistham |  
bhaktābhyāṃ puṣpamālyaṃ sahayugagirijaṃ dhārayantaṃ vṛṣasthaṃ  
  
p. 181)  
  
succhatraṃ caṇḍakarṇe suravaravinutaṃ caṇḍanāthaṃ bhaje'ham || 31 ||  
  
|| dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ ||  
  
hutavahamaṇikośaṃ jñānamudrākarāgrai  
sitamapi dadhataṃ lambitaṃ savyapādam |  
śayitamaparapādaṃ bhūtasaṃsthaṃ triṇetraṃ  
girivaranirakasthaṃ dakṣiṇāmūrtimīḍe || 32 ||  
  
|| yogadakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ ||  
  
cinmudrāmakṣamālāṃ paraśumapikarai savyavāme vahantaṃ  
vāme bhāge ca jānuṃ parinihitakaraṃ yogapaṭṭāvṛtāṅgam |  
savyelambyāṅghripadmaṃ sanakamukhayutaṃ bhūtapṛṣṭhasthapādaṃ   
śāntaṃ traikṣaṃ prasannaṃ girivarasahitaṃ dakṣiṇāmūrtimīḍe || 33 ||  
  
|| vīṇādakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ ||  
  
dhavalaruciragātraṃ sarparājopavītaṃ śaśidharamathavahniṃ cākṣamālāṃ   
vahantam |  
sphuritakanakavīṇā kiñcitākuñcitāṅghri girivaraśikharasthaṃ   
dakṣiṇāmūrtidaivam || 3 ||  
  
|| kālāntakadhyānam ||  
  
nīlābhaṃ raktanetraṃ jvalitakacadharaṃ krūradaṃṣṭraṃ subhīmaṃ   
śūlaṃ bāṇañca khaḍgaṃ paraśumavitanuṃ kheṭakaṃ pāśamīḍam |  
  
p. 182)  
  
sūcīhastañca savye paraśukaranikare bibhrataṃ kālakaṇṭhaṃ   
dhvaṃsadvāmāṅghri padmaṃ munijamṛtiharaṃ kālakālannamāmi || 35 ||  
  
|| kāmāriḥ ||  
  
bhasmoddhūlita vigrahaṃ śaśidharaṃ veṇījaṭāmaṇḍitaṃ   
ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgau dadhānamamalaṃ vīrāsane saṃsthitam |  
arkesavyataloparītaratalaṃ vinyassayogeparaṃ

|| lakulīśaḥ ||  
  
śoṇāṅgaṃ ḍamaruñca śūlamapare vame'bhayaṃ kuṇṭhikāṃ  
bibhrāṇasmita bhasmarāśitanuṃ piṅgordhvakeśāvṛtam |  
tryakṣaṃ nīlagalaṃ mahoragadharaṃ hārādibhūṣojvalaṃ   
dhyāyāme lakulīśvaraṃ surapatiṃ padmāsanasthaṃ hṛdi || 37 ||  
  
|| bhairavaḥ ||  
  
raktajvālajaṭādharaṃ triṇayanaṃ daṃṣṭrākarālānvitaṃ   
haste pāśakapālaśūlaḍamaruṃ dakṣe'nyato vibhratam |  
ghaṇṭādāmasamena jaṃghamamalaṃ   
taṃ kṣetrapālaṃ bhaje || * * * * * * * * *   
  
p. 183)  
  
|| āpaduddhāraṇam ||  
  
udyadbhāskarasannibhantriṇayanaṃ pullollasatkumbhakaṃ  
phalaṃ daṇḍakapālapāṇiyugalaṃ tāṭaṅkakarṇadvayam |  
haryakṣājina kañcukaṃ misananaṃ janvantakāntakarṇam  
ghaṇṭādāmakṛtopavītamaniśaṃ naumyāpaduddhāraṇam || 39 ||  
  
|| vaṭukaḥ ||  
  
karakalitakapālaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ daṇḍapāṇiṃ taruṇatimiranīlodavyālayajñopavītam |  
kṛtasyaparijyā vighnavidhvaṃsahetuṃ jayatu vaṭukanāthaṃ siddhidaṃ

|| kṣetrapālaḥ ||

|| vīrabhadraḥ ||

|| dakṣayajñaharaḥ ||

paścādvāma padāmbujārulasatāṃ śuṣṭha?sthitaṃ bhāvayet

|| gurumūrtiḥ ||

|| jalaṃdharāriḥ ||

|| ekapādatrimūrtidhyānam ||

|| ekapādaḥ ||

|| gaurīvarapradānadhyānam ||

|| cakradānam ||

|| gaurilīlāsamanvita dhyānam ||

|| viṣāpaharaṇaḥ ||

|| brahmaśiraśchedaḥ ||

|| kūrmasaṃhāradhyānam ||

|| matsyasaṃhāriḥ ||

p. 188)

|| varāhāriḥ ||  
  
hemābhaṃ jvālakeśaṃ kuṭilaganayanaṃ bhairavākāradehaṃ

sevatve dhārayantaṃ nikaṭanarahariḥ taṃ varāhaghnamīḍe || 59 ||  
  
|| prārthanāmūrtidhyānam ||  
  
kundābhaṃ trivilocanaṃ śaśidharaṃ taṃ pātu ṭaṅkaṃ dadhat |  
dakṣāṃbaddhajaṭāgra jānutalayo vāme tu caṇḍapriyam |  
āliṅgyekakareṇa taccibukato nyastānya pāṇipriyaṃ  
jalpan pātuśivo naḥ prārthanāvigraham || 60 ||  
  
|| raktabhikṣāṭanaḥ ||  
  
kaṭyākārantu savye phaṇipatidadhataṃ vāmahaste tu pāśaṃ   
vāme bhikṣākapālaṃ parakarakamalenonnamayyatriśūlam |

vande devaṃ maheśaṃ munisuravinutaṃ raktabhikṣāṭanegam || 61 ||  
  
|| śiṣyabhāvadhyānam ||  
  
p. 189)

ṭaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dadhānaṃ guruguhapurato yastalemamṛtamūrtiṃ  
tadvācyomardhatattvaṃ hariyutagirijaṃ śiṣyabhāveśamīḍe || 62 ||  
  
|| aghorāstram ||  
  
raktavastradharandevaṃ bhinnāñjana samaprabham |  
bṛhadbhujāṣṭakopetaṃ ūrdhvakeśa sudaṃṣṭriṇam ||  
  
spaṣṭadaṣṭamarāṣṭhañca dīptāgni samalocanam |  
kiṅkaṇīmālikopetaṃ pādau nūpurasaṃyutam ||  
  
saptāyudhasamāyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |  
mekhalodarakaṇṭheṣu karṇayobāhubhistathā ||  
  
pādayorhastayoścaivā nāgabhūṣaṃ caturdaśi |  
śuklayajñopavītañcā raktapuṣpopaśobhitam ||  
  
paṅkajāsanamadhyasthaṃ triṇetraṃ snigdhamaṅgalam |  
śūlaṃ musalabhetālaṃ khaḍgaṃ ḍamarukaṃ karaiḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇetarabibhrāṇaṃ vāmakaiśūlamadhyamaḥ |  
ghaṇṭākheṭakapālañca vāmapādaṃ purassaram ||  
  
p. 190)  
  
yānamārgasthiraṃ ghoraṃ somasūryāgnilocanam |  
kurvāṇaṃ sādhakantrāṇāṃ kaṭakākṣaitriṇāghuṇaiḥ ||

dhyāyet tīrthāghorāstraḥ samastaduritāntakam || 63 ||  
  
|| aṣṭādhyakṣasūtradhyānam ||

stridiharakaluṣāṃ pādamekannidhāya |

prāṇaṃ paśyantriṇetraṃ vitaratuvipulaṃ dakṣiṇāmūrtidevam || 64 ||  
  
|| sundaramūrtiḥ ||

|| appar ||

|| gaṇapatimūlamantram ||

|| subrahmaṇyam ||

|| devi ||

|| vāmādyaṣṭaśaktiḥ ||

indrādyaṣṭamūrtaye namaḥ |  
oṃ suṃ somāya namaḥ |  
oṃ yūṃ aṃgārakāya namaḥ |  
oṃ budhāya namaḥ |  
oṃ buṃ bṛhaspataye namaḥ |  
oṃ śaṃ śanaiścarāya namaḥ |  
oṃ raṃ rāhave namaḥ |  
oṃ kaṃ ketave namaḥ |  
  
|| indrādyaṣṭamūlamantram ||  
  
oṃ iṃ indrāya namaḥ |  
oṃ aṃ agnaye namaḥ |  
oṃ yamāya namaḥ |  
oṃ niṃ nir-ṛtaye namaḥ |  
oṃ vaṃ varuṇāya namaḥ |  
oṃ vaṃ vāyave namaḥ |  
oṃ kaṃ kuberāya namaḥ |  
oṃ īṃ īśānāya namaḥ |  
oṃ kaṃ brahmaṇe namaḥ |  
  
sṛṣṭi-  
  
prajā prajāpatirvedā vidhātā ca pitāmahaḥ |  
ajā sṛṣṭiścaturvaktrairbrahmādyāścāṣṭamūrtayaḥ ||  
  
oṃ hīṃ viṣṇave namaḥ |  
  
p. 194)  
  
saṃkarṣaṇaśca pradyumnānurūḍhapuruṣottama |  
adhokṣajāvāsudeva nāmaśca nārasiṃhaśca vāmanāścāṣṭa mūrtayaḥ |  
  
|| dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ ||  
  
onnamo bhagavate dakṣiṇāmūrtaye mahyaṃ medhāṃ prayacchāmi svāhā |  
  
|| agastyādyaṣṭamūrtayaḥ ||  
  
durge-  
  
oṃ maṃ durge rakṣaṇe svāhā |  
durgākātyāyanīdyaṣṭa parivāraḥ ||  
  
|| somāskandandaḥ ||  
  
oṃ hāṃ vyomavyāpine śrī kaṇṭhāyanamaḥ |  
  
|| anantādyaṣṭavidyeśvaraḥ ||  
  
|| naṭeśar ||  
  
oṃ hāṃ sakṣamalavarayūṃ tumburānanta bhairavāya svāhā |  
  
|| anantādi ||  
  
oṃ hāṃ caṃ caṇḍeśvarāya namaḥ | indrādiḥ | kṣetrapālaḥ |  
oṃ kṣāṃ kṣīṃ kṣūṃ kṣetrapālāyanamaḥ | oṃ haṃ saṃkṣaṃ maṃ lūṃ yūṃ   
tripurānta bhairavāya namaḥ |  
  
asitāṅgoruruścaṇḍa krodhaśconmattabhairavaḥ |  
  
p. 195)  
  
kapālibhīṣaṇaścaivā saṃhāraścāṣṭabhairavaḥ |  
  
|| aghorāstrar ||  
  
oṃ śrīṃ sphurasphuraprasphuraprasphura ghoraghoratanurūpa   
caṭacaṭapracaṭapracaṭa kahakaha vamavama badhayabadhaya ghātaya ghātaya   
aghorāstrāya huṃ phaṭ svāhā |  
  
dāruṇaṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ raudrāṣṭamūrtiḥ | pāśupatāstram |  
oṃ śīṃ paṃ śuṃ huṃphaṭ pāśupatāstrāyanamaḥ |  
indrādyaṣṭa vidyeśvaraḥ | reṇukādevi |  
oṃ hauṃ svāhā | bhagavate raktapañcami reṇukādevī-  
dahadaha paca paca sarvajanavaśaṃ kuru kuru svāhā |  
jayā ca vijayā caiva bhonī mohinī tathā ||  
  
malinī mālinī caiva bhoginī bhogavatyathāṣṭadārumūrtayaḥ |  
  
|| bhadrakāliḥ ||  
  
oṃ bhaṃ bhadrakālyai namaḥ | vāmādyaṣṭaśaktiḥ | cāmuṇḍā |  
oṃ hāṃ hrīṃ hrauṃ sarvātmane cāmuṇḍāyai namaḥ |  
bhadrakālyai ca maṇḍūkacacchaṭābhairavīstathā |  
cāmuṇḍyai varmiṇīcaikāla rātryai tu kālikādyaṣṭamūrtayaḥ ||  
  
p. 196)  
  
|| saptamātṛ ||  
  
brāhmī māheśvarī caivā kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā |  
vārāhi caiva māhendri cāmuṇḍasaptamātaraḥ ||  
  
oṃ śrīṃ hrīṃ brāhmai namaḥ |  
indrāṇi māheśvarī caivā vaiṣṇavī vārāhī tathā |  
cāmuṇḍibhadrakālī ca durgāyai vīrabhadrayoḥ ||  
  
|| balipīṭham ||  
  
avighnañcaṇḍyakumbhe tu āmodaṃ pūrvakumbhake |  
pramodaṃ yāmyakumbhe tu sumukhaṃ vāruṇe ghaṭe ||  
  
durmukhaṃ saumyakumbhantu vighnakartāramīśake |  
anuktaṃ sarvadevānāṃ * * * * * * * * |  
  
indrādi sarvaśaktiḥ | śivasāvitri |  
vyomavyomāyavidmahe sūkṣmasūkṣmāya dhīmahi |  
tannorudraḥ pracodayāt | śivagāyatri | tanmaheśāya vidmahe  
vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi | tannorudraḥ pracodayāt |  
  
pratyaṅgirimūlam | oṃ saṃbhakṣajvālā jihvākarāladaṃṣṭrāṃ-  
  
प्। १९७)  
  
प्रत्यङ्गिरास्त्रम् । आं ईं ऊं रुद्रास्थि शृङ्खले ।  
हुं सर्वतोभद्रे कुटिलरुद्रवचन विदारिरक्षमाम् ।  
  
प्रत्यङ्गिरे धाम धाम ज्योति ज्योतिस्सुवस्सुवर्भुवोर्भुवो-  
वाह्य मृतोहं सत्यहं त्रिभिदन् पादुजुषां लक्ष्मीं-  
नमो वः किरिकेयं करोतिममेवा ।  
  
विशतु महादेव सुवृते नमोनमस्स्वाहा ।  
  
॥ सदाशिवाक्षरम् ॥  
  
ॐ हौं हं सदाशिवाय नमः । नवाक्षरम् । हौं हं सं मं क्षं रं   
नं यं मं शिवाय नमः ।  
  
॥ देवि ॥  
  
ॐ क्षां क्षिं क्षूं क्षौं उमायै नमः ।  
  
॥ गङ्गागायत्रि ॥  
  
ॐ अम्बरीषायविद्महे सिन्धुद्वीपायधीमहि । तन्नो गङ्गा प्रचोदयात् ।  
  
॥ पञ्चाक्षरम् ॥  
  
हौ सं शिवाय शिवमन्त्रं हां हौ हं सः ।  
आमोदश्च प्रमोदश्च सुमुखो दुर्मुखस्तथा ।  
  
प्। १९८)  
  
अविघ्नो विघ्नराजश्च पक्ष्याशी पञ्चहस्तकः ।  
  
॥ शास्ताध्यानम् ॥  
  
कल्हारोज्वल नीलकुन्तलधरं कालाम्बुद श्यामलं  
कर्पूराकलिकाभिराम कलिका कुन्देन्दुबिम्बानना ।  
श्री दण्डाङ्कुशशूलविलसत् पाणि सुह्री धारहं  
रम्यशत्रुविमर्दनं हृदि महाशास्तेशमाद्यं भजे ॥ १ ॥  
  
॥ पुनः ॥  
  
खड्गं बाणं त्रिशूलं भिन्धिपालं त्रिणेत्रं   
रक्ताङ्गं हेमबद्धं मरकत वर्णमारङ्गदीप्यम् ।  
दिव्याम्बुमालां द्वितिनिभवरदां द्विद्वियां वीरशौर्यां  
प्राणे वा शक्तिसहितं हरिहरतनयं शाश्वतं शास्तमूर्तिम् ॥ २ ॥  
  
॥ शास्ताशक्तिपूर्णाध्यानम् ॥  
  
श्यामान्द्विनेत्रां सुगन्धिसूतुं भुजद्वये पद्मसरोजहस्ते ।  
सव्ये तु लम्ब्याशयने तु वामे पद्मं करण्डं मकुटञ्च पूर्णम् ॥ ३ ॥  
  
॥ पुष्कलै ॥  
  
अम्बा च पुत्रीं द्विभुजां द्विनेत्रां सव्योत्पलामूरु च वामहस्ता ।  
वामे तु लम्बा उदरे तु शय्यां करण्डकं पुष्कलपीतवर्णाम् ॥ ४ ॥  
  
प्। १९९)  
  
॥ शास्ता ॥  
  
श्यामवर्णशरीर सुयौवनं तुङ्गपङ्कजसहस्रकुन्दलम् ।  
योगवेष्टित पद्मसुखासनं वामदक्षिण पुष्कलपूर्णयोः ॥  
  
ॐ श्रीं ह्रीं क्लीं हरिहरपुत्राय अर्थलाभाय शत्रुनाशनाय  
पुत्रलाभाय मदगजवाहनाय श्रीमहाशास्ताय नमः ।  
गजध्वजाय विद्महे शृणिहस्तायधीमहि तन्नो शास्ता प्रचोदयात् ॥ ५ ॥  
  
॥ पूर्णैपुष्कलै ॥  
  
पूर्णञ्च दक्षिणे स्थित्वा पुष्कलां वामपार्श्वतः ।  
पूर्णां वै कनकाभासां श्यामाभां पुष्कलां स्मृताम् ॥  
  
द्विनेत्रां द्विभुजां सौम्यां सर्वाभरणभूषिताम् ।  
दिव्यगन्धानुलिप्ताङ्गौ दिव्यमालानुभूषिताम् ॥  
  
श्यामवर्णधरां पूर्णां पुष्कलां कनकाम्बराम् ।  
पूर्णां वामकरे पुष्पं दक्षिणे कटन्विताम् ॥  
  
कुञ्चितं वाम पादे तु दक्षिणे लम्बितं भवेत् ।  
सिंहकुण्डलमेवोक्तं तथा मकरकुण्डलम् ॥  
  
पुष्कलं दक्षिणे पुष्पं वामे वै वरदं भवेत् ।  
वामे तु लम्बितं पादं दक्षिणेन तु कुञ्चितम् ॥  
  
प्। २००)  
  
सङ्कुकर्णयुतं वापि तथा वै सिंहकुण्डलम् ।  
  
॥ अक्षतलिङ्गध्यानम् ॥  
  
कृष्णवर्णन्त्रिणेत्रञ्च हारकेयूरधारिणम् ।  
चतुर्भुजसमायुक्तं पादनूपुरसंयुतम् ॥  
  
खड्गखेटधनुर्बाणं धारयन्तं महाबलम् ।  
एवमर्घ्यस्वरूपन्तु तत्तद्रूपं विचिन्तयेत् ॥ १ ॥  
  
॥ पुष्पलिङ्गम् ॥  
  
सौम्यं सौम्येक्षणोपेतं चतुर्हस्त समायुतम् ।  
विद्युन्मालानिभञ्चैव जटामकुटमण्डितम् ॥  
  
दक्षेऽभयाक्षमालाभि इतरे वरपाशयुक् ।  
  
॥ अन्नलिङ्गम् ॥  
  
शूलमूलाभये दक्षे शूलाग्रे वरतेतरः ।  
रौद्रदृष्टिज्वलत्केश व्यक्तास्यं करशूलकम् ॥  
  
॥ पुनरपि ॥  
  
शुक्लवस्त्रधरन्देवं शुक्लमाल्याविभूषितम् ।  
सर्वाभरणसंयुक्तं चतुर्दोर्भिः समन्वितम् ॥  
  
हस्ते पात्रधरन्दक्षे वामे नीलोत्पलन्तथा ।  
  
प्। २०१)  
  
हरिणं परशुञ्चोर्ध्वे धारयन्तं भुजद्वये ।  
अन्नलिङ्गस्वरूपन्तु सर्वकामफलप्रदम् ॥ ४ ॥  
  
कुमुदं कुमुदाक्षञ्च पुण्डरीकोऽथवा मतः ।  
शङ्कुकर्णसर्वनेत्र सुप्रतिष्ठितः ॥  
  
भवश्शर्वश्च रुद्रश्च महादेवश्च भीमकः ।  
उग्रः पशुपतिश्चैवा ईशान्यत्वाष्टमूर्तयः ॥ ५ ॥  
  
देवि दीपाराधनै पूजादेवतै ॐ ह्रीं अम्ब्यै नमः ।  
गणाम्बिकायै नमः । श्रियै नमः । धारिकायै नमः ।  
वाग्विन्यै नमः । ॐ ह्लां निवृत्तिकलायै नमः ।  
प्रतिष्ठाकलायै नमः । विद्या कलायै नमः । शान्तिकलायै नमः ।  
ॐ हौं शान्त्यतीत कलायै नमः ।  
तत्त्वत्रयं पादशिरेण कुक्षिं दलेषु वामादिषु शक्तिभिश्च ।  
नालञ्च गौरिज्वलनञ्च रुद्रं कुम्भादि पूजामिति शम्बरैश्च ॥  
  
॥ सप्तमाता गायत्रि ॥  
  
सर्वशक्ती च विद्महे सप्तरूपाय धीमहि । तन्नो मातरः प्रचोदयात् ॥  
  
॥ विघ्नेश्वरगायत्रि ॥  
  
प्। २०२)  
  
तत्पुरुषाय विद्महे वक्त्रकुण्डाय धीमहि ।  
तन्नो दन्तिः प्रचोदयात् ।  
  
॥ सुब्रह्मण्य गायत्रि ॥  
  
विशाखाय विद्महे बाणहस्ताय धीमहि । तन्नस्कन्दः प्रचोदयात् ॥  
  
॥ ज्येष्ठागायत्रि ॥  
  
फलप्रदायविद्महे पापहारी च धीमहि ।  
  
तन्नो ज्येष्ठः प्रचोदयात् ।  
  
॥ दुर्गीगायत्रि ॥  
  
कात्यायनी च विद्महे बाणहायधीमहि ।  
तन्नो दुर्गी प्रचोदयात् ।  
  
॥ सूर्यगायत्रि ॥  
  
अश्वध्वजाय विद्महे पद्महस्ताय धीमहि ।  
  
तन्नो सूर्यप्रचोदयात् ।  
  
॥ रथध्यानम् ॥  
  
चक्रञ्च सूर्यचन्द्रञ्च पश्चाद्ब्रह्ममयं भवेत् ।  
तत्पश्चात्पीठमेवं स्यात् विष्णुशैलगजन्तथा ॥  
  
प्। २०३)  
  
सर्वदेवेषु पादञ्च तत्पश्चाद्भूवरन्तथा ।  
नक्षत्ररन्ध्रमेवं स्यात् नागञ्च सूत्रबन्धनम् ।  
तत्कर्तुं रुद्रमेवस्यात् ध्यात्वा देवत्थन्तथा ॥  
  
॥ त्रिशूलास्त्रध्यानम् ॥  
  
त्रिशूलम्-  
  
शूलास्रमध्यपत्रे तु रुद्रं निष्कलमेव च ।  
ब्रह्माणं सव्यपत्रे तु विष्णुञ्च वामपत्रके ॥  
  
तस्याधश्चतुरश्रञ्च मध्ये च पार्वतीं तथा ।  
सव्ये सरस्वतीञ्चैव महालक्ष्मीञ्च वामके ॥  
  
चन्द्रसूर्यद्वयं पार्श्वं अधस्य सर्वदेवता ।  
कुम्भे उडुपदेवत्यं दण्डस्य भुवनन्तथा ॥  
  
पञ्चावृतस्य पादाश्रं शूलास्त्रं ध्यायेद्गुरुः ।  
  
॥ गोपुरध्यानम् ॥  
  
द्वारञ्च ब्रह्मदेवत्यं निला विष्णुस्तथैव च ।  
नालं कुम्भेषु रुद्रञ्च शिला इष्टिञ्च दारुकैः ॥  
  
सर्वदेव-ऋषींश्चैव सुधैरसञ्च शक्तिषु ।  
सर्व तन्त्र विधानञ्च भक्तैश्च गणभूतकैः ॥  
  
शृङ्गारञ्च अलङ्कृत्य नक्षत्रञ्च समाचरेत् ।  
  
प्। २०४)  
  
इति गोपुररूपन्तु नेत्रञ्च शिरनासिषु ।  
इत्यावाह्यासु सम्पूज्याः * * * * * * * * *   
।  
  
॥ सप्तमाताब्राह्मिध्यानम् ॥  
  
ब्राह्मी तु पीतवर्णं स्यात् हंसवाहनमेव चा ।  
चतुर्भुजान्त्रिणेत्राञ्च चतुर्वक्त्रन्तथैव च ॥  
  
अभयं वरदञ्चैव अक्षमाला च कुण्डिकाम् ।  
सर्वाभरणसंयुक्तां जटामकुटमण्डिताम् ॥ १ ॥  
  
॥ माहेश्वरि ॥  
  
चतुर्भुजन्त्रिणेत्रञ्च शुक्लवर्णं समायुतम् ।  
जटामकुटसंयुक्तां एकवक्त्रसमन्विताम् ॥  
  
अभयं वरदञ्चैव पद्मं सव्यञ्च धारिणम् ।  
वाहनं वृषभं कृत्वा माहेश्वरीं तथैव चा ॥ २ ॥  
  
॥ कौमारि ॥  
  
एकवक्त्रन्द्विनेत्रञ्च नीलवर्णन्तथैव चा ।  
चतुर्भुजसमायुक्तां द्विपादञ्च समन्विताम् ॥  
मयूरवाहनारूढां जटामकुटमण्डिताम् ।  
अपरे वज्रशक्तिञ्च अभयं वरदन्तथा ॥ ३ ॥  
  
प्। २०५)  
  
॥ वैष्णवि ॥  
  
द्विनेत्रां चतुर्भुजां शान्तां श्यामवर्ण सुयौवनाम् ।  
शङ्खचक्रधरां कृत्वा अभयं वरदान्विताम् ॥ ४ ॥  
  
वाहनं गरुडं कृत्वा सर्वाभरणभूषिताम् ।  
  
॥ वाराहि ॥  
  
चतुर्भुजान्त्रिणेत्राञ्च पीताम्बरधरायुताम् ।  
वराहरूपसंयुक्तां रक्तवर्णसमन्विताम् ॥  
  
किरीटमकुटोपेतां हेमनीलस्वरूपिणीम् ।  
स रत्नमकुटोपेतां हंसवाहनमेव चा ॥ ५ ॥  
   
हसलामुसलञ्चैव अभयं वरदन्तथा ।  
  
माहेन्द्रीं द्विनेत्राञ्चतुर्भुजां शान्तां अभयं वरदन्तथा ।  
वज्रशक्तिधरोपेतां हैमनीलस्वरूपिकाम् ॥ ६ ॥  
  
सरत्नमकुटोपेतां गजवाहनमेव च ॥ ६ ॥  
  
॥ चामुण्डि ॥  
  
चतुर्भुजान्त्रिणेत्राञ्च कालमेघस्वरूपिणीम् ।  
चामुण्डिं कारयेद्धीमान् कालमेघसमप्रभाम् ॥  
  
कपालशूलसंयुक्तां पाशं डमरुकन्तथा ।  
  
  
  
  
मुक्तबोद्ह इन्दोलोगिचल् रेसेअर्च्ह् इन्स्तितुते©२०११ मुक्तबोध इन्दोलोगिचल् रेसेअर्छ् इन्स्तितुते  अल्ल् रिघ्त्स् रेसेर्वेद्।ए-तेxत्स् मय् बे विएwएद् ओन्ल्य् ओन्लिने ओर् दोwन्लोअदेद् ड़ोर् प्रिवते स्तुद्य्।ए-तेxत्स् मय् नोत्, उन्देर् अन्य् चिर्चुम्स्तन्चेस्, बे चोपिएद्, रेपुब्लिस्हेद्,रेप्रोदुचेद्, दिस्त्रिबुतेद् ओर् सोल्द्, एइथेर् इन् ओरिगिनल् ओर् अल्तेरेद् ड़ोर्म्, wइथोउत्थे एxप्रेस्स् पेर्मिस्सिओन् ओड़् मुक्तबोध इन्दोलोगिचल् रेसेअर्छ् इन्स्तितुते इन् wरितिन्ग्।दत-एन्तेरेद् ब्य् थे स्तड़्ड़् ओड़् मुक्तबोध उन्देर् थे दिरेच्तिओन् ओड़् मर्क् स्। ग्। द्य्च्ज़्कोwस्कि।
